## Prompt:
07/04/2026, 21:04:58

full wireframe spec for every screen

## Response:
07/04/2026, 21:04:59

I’m turning the product spec into a screen-by-screen wireframe package: layout regions, components, states, and primary actions. I’ll cover learner screens first, then admin screens, so it is usable by design and engineering immediately.

> Thought for a few seconds

Below is the **full wireframe specification for every screen** in the app.

This is a **low-fidelity product wireframe spec**, not visual design. It defines:

*   screen purpose
*   layout structure
*   UI components
*   user actions
*   states
*   navigation
*   content rules

It is intended for:

*   UX designer
*   UI designer
*   frontend developer
*   product manager

* * *

1\. Wireframe conventions
=========================

Device assumptions
------------------

Primary target:

*   mobile portrait
*   375–430 px width phone layout

Secondary:

*   larger phones and tablets adapt from same structure

Layout zones used in spec
-------------------------

Each screen is described using:

*   **Header**
*   **Body**
*   **Footer**
*   **Bottom navigation**
*   **Overlay / modal**, where needed

Core component naming
---------------------

*   Primary button
*   Secondary button
*   Audio button
*   Slow audio button
*   Mic button
*   Card
*   Progress bar
*   Chip
*   Toggle
*   Bottom sheet
*   Toast
*   Modal
*   Empty state
*   Loading state
*   Error state

Interaction principles
----------------------

*   one dominant action per screen
*   replay audio always easy to find
*   Thai support always visible or one tap away
*   mic actions large and centered when speaking is required

* * *

2\. App-wide shell
==================

2.1 Global mobile frame
-----------------------

All learner screens share:

### Safe area

*   top inset respected
*   bottom inset respected

### Standard header pattern

Left:

*   back button or logo

Center:

*   screen title

Right:

*   optional settings/help/exit

### Standard bottom navigation

Tabs:

*   Home
*   Review
*   Sounds
*   Speak
*   Profile

Behavior:

*   highlight current tab
*   preserve navigation stack per tab where practical

### Global overlays

Used across app:

*   mic permission modal
*   download content modal
*   streak celebration modal
*   lesson completion modal
*   retry audio modal

* * *

3\. Learner app screens
=======================

* * *

3.1 Splash screen
=================

Purpose
-------

*   show brand
*   initialize app
*   check auth/session
*   preload essential config

Layout
------

### Header

None

### Body

Centered vertically:

*   app logo
*   app name
*   short subtitle: “Learn simple English by listening and speaking”
*   loading indicator

### Footer

*   version text
*   privacy / terms small links optional

Actions
-------

None

States
------

### Loading

*   spinner active

### Error

*   “Something went wrong”
*   Retry button

Navigation
----------

*   if first open → Language Selection
*   if returning signed-in user → Home
*   if returning guest with session → Home

* * *

3.2 Language selection screen
=============================

Purpose
-------

Set interface language for learner

Layout
------

### Header

*   title: “Choose Language”

### Body

Top:

*   short instruction text

Middle:  
Three large language cards:

*   Thai
*   English
*   Bilingual

Each card includes:

*   label
*   sample text preview
*   checkmark when selected

Bottom:

*   primary button: Continue

### Footer

*   small “Can change later in Settings”

Actions
-------

*   select language
*   continue

States
------

### Default

*   Thai preselected

### Disabled continue

*   only if no option selected

Navigation
----------

Continue → Welcome / Onboarding Intro

* * *

3.3 Welcome / onboarding intro
==============================

Purpose
-------

Explain app learning method simply

Layout
------

### Header

*   skip button on right

### Body

Swipeable onboarding carousel, 3 slides

#### Slide 1

*   illustration
*   heading: Listen first
*   text: Hear sounds and repeat slowly

#### Slide 2

*   illustration
*   heading: Speak every day
*   text: Practice with your voice in short lessons

#### Slide 3

*   illustration
*   heading: Learn useful English
*   text: Use words for food, home, family, and daily life

Below slides:

*   page indicators

### Footer

*   primary button: Continue
*   secondary text button: Skip

Actions
-------

*   swipe slides
*   continue
*   skip

Navigation
----------

Continue/Skip → Account Setup

* * *

3.4 Account setup screen
========================

Purpose
-------

Create learner profile and preferences

Layout
------

### Header

*   back button
*   title: “About You”

### Body

Vertical form with large spacing:

*   Name input
*   Native language dropdown
*   Learning goal chips:
    *   Daily life
    *   Home conversation
    *   Travel
    *   Start from zero
*   Learning pace chips:
    *   Slow
    *   Normal
*   Optional reminder time selector

### Footer

*   primary button: Continue

Actions
-------

*   fill fields
*   choose goal
*   choose pace
*   choose reminder time

States
------

### Validation

*   name required or allow skip to “Learner”

Navigation
----------

Continue → Level Check

* * *

3.5 Level check screen
======================

Purpose
-------

Quickly determine starting level

Layout
------

### Header

*   back button
*   title: “Start Level”

### Body

Stacked cards:

#### Card 1: Understand words?

*   Hear “water”
*   Buttons:
    *   I understand
    *   I do not understand

#### Card 2: Can you say your name in English?

*   prompt text
*   mic button
*   skip option

#### Card 3: Repeat simple word

*   play “hello”
*   big mic button
*   status chip after attempt

Below:

*   short note: “This helps us choose the right starting point.”

### Footer

*   primary button: See My Starting Lesson
*   text button: Skip Test

Actions
-------

*   listen
*   answer yes/no
*   record speech
*   skip

System behavior
---------------

For beginner audience:

*   likely assign Level 0 or Week 1 Lesson 1

Navigation
----------

Continue → Onboarding Results / Home

* * *

3.6 Onboarding result screen
============================

Purpose
-------

Show where learner starts

Layout
------

### Header

*   title: “You’re Ready”

### Body

Centered card:

*   level badge: Beginner Start
*   recommended start: Lesson 1
*   short message:  
    “We will begin with sounds, small words, and short sentences.”

Secondary card:

*   what you will do today
    *   listen
    *   repeat
    *   say 5 words
    *   practice 1 mini dialogue

### Footer

*   primary button: Start First Lesson

Navigation
----------

Start → Home or directly Lesson 1

* * *

3.7 Home screen
===============

Purpose
-------

Main dashboard and entry point

Layout
------

### Header

Left:

*   greeting: “Hello, Mali”

Right:

*   streak badge
*   settings icon optional

### Body

Scrollable vertical dashboard

#### Section 1: Today’s lesson card

Large featured card:

*   lesson number/title
*   estimated time
*   progress ring
*   “Continue” or “Start”
*   one-line summary of content

#### Section 2: Review due today

Smaller card row:

*   count of words due
*   count of sounds due
*   CTA: Review Now

#### Section 3: Pronunciation shortcut

Card:

*   title: Practice Sounds
*   subtitle: R/L, V/W, TH, final sounds
*   button: Start Practice

#### Section 4: Recent words

Horizontal chips/cards:

*   water
*   rice
*   help
*   mother  
    Each with mini mastery indicator

#### Section 5: Progress summary

*   lessons completed
*   words learned
*   current streak

#### Section 6: Recommended next action

System-generated card:

*   “Practice water again”  
    or
*   “Review final consonants”

### Bottom navigation

Visible

Actions
-------

*   continue lesson
*   start review
*   open pronunciation practice
*   open recent word
*   navigate tabs

States
------

### New learner

*   only Today’s Lesson prominent
*   no recent words yet

### Returning learner

*   resume progress visible

### Empty review

*   show “No review due today”

* * *

3.8 Lesson map / course progress screen
=======================================

Purpose
-------

Show overall curriculum structure

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   title: “Course”

### Body

Vertical level/module list:

*   Week 1
*   Week 2
*   Week 3  
    Each as expandable accordion or stacked cards

Inside each week card:

*   lesson rows
*   completion checkmarks
*   locked/unlocked states
*   review day highlighted

### Footer

None

Actions
-------

*   expand week
*   tap unlocked lesson
*   view completed lesson again

States
------

*   locked lessons dimmed
*   current lesson highlighted

Navigation
----------

Tap lesson → Lesson Intro or Lesson Player

* * *

3.9 Lesson intro screen
=======================

Purpose
-------

Prepare user before lesson starts

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   title: lesson number

### Body

Main lesson card:

*   lesson title
*   sound focus
*   5 target words preview
*   sentence pattern preview
*   estimated time

Secondary area:

*   what you will practice:
    *   listen
    *   repeat
    *   speak
    *   mini dialogue

### Footer

*   primary button: Start Lesson
*   secondary button: Download audio optional

Actions
-------

*   start lesson
*   preview words
*   optional download

Navigation
----------

Start → Lesson Player

* * *

3.10 Lesson player screen
=========================

This is the core screen. It changes based on step type.

Purpose
-------

Guide learner through one lesson step by step

Global layout
-------------

### Header

Left:

*   close/back button

Center:

*   lesson title or step label

Right:

*   help icon
*   lesson progress percent optional

Below header:

*   horizontal progress bar

### Body

Dynamic content area, centered and scroll-safe

### Footer

Always fixed:

*   replay audio button
*   slow audio button
*   mic button or next button depending on step
*   next/continue button

* * *

3.10A Listen-only step
----------------------

### Body

*   large target text or sound symbol
*   optional picture
*   Thai hint under it
*   one clear instruction: “Listen”
*   waveform / speaker icon animation on play

### Footer

*   replay
*   slow audio
*   next

### Actions

*   play audio
*   replay
*   continue

* * *

3.10B Repeat-after-me step
--------------------------

### Body

*   target word or sentence large
*   Thai translation smaller
*   pronunciation hint beneath
*   optional mouth hint icon

Below:

*   instruction: “Listen and say it”

Recording area:

*   big mic button
*   after recording, show playback chip

### Footer

*   replay
*   slow audio
*   big mic
*   continue when attempt done

### States

*   idle
*   listening
*   recording
*   processing
*   feedback received

* * *

3.10C Syllable drill step
-------------------------

### Body

*   word at top
*   syllable split shown as separate capsules  
    Example: WA / ter
*   clap or stress hint optional

Below:

*   tap syllable to hear
*   “say each part” instruction

### Footer

*   replay
*   mic
*   next

### Actions

*   tap syllable
*   hear full word
*   speak syllables
*   continue

* * *

3.10D Word flashcard step
-------------------------

### Body

Centered card:

*   image
*   English word
*   Thai meaning
*   pronunciation hint
*   syllable split

Below card:

*   play normal
*   play slow
*   favorite toggle optional

### Footer

*   previous word
*   next word
*   mic to repeat

### Variants

*   one word per screen
*   or swipeable word carousel

* * *

3.10E Meaning match step
------------------------

### Body

Top:

*   audio prompt only or word prompt

Middle:

*   3 or 4 large answer cards
    *   Thai meaning choices  
        or
    *   picture choices

### Footer

None until answer chosen, then:

*   continue button

### States

*   unanswered
*   correct highlighted
*   incorrect highlighted with correct answer reveal

* * *

3.10F Speak sentence step
-------------------------

### Body

*   sentence large
*   Thai translation underneath
*   key target word highlighted
*   optional speaker icon beside sentence

Recording section:

*   large mic button
*   live state label:
    *   tap to speak
    *   listening
    *   processing

After attempt:

*   transcript box
*   feedback chip
*   retry option

### Footer

*   replay
*   slow audio
*   mic
*   continue

* * *

3.10G Question-answer step
--------------------------

### Body

Top:

*   app asks spoken question
*   question text visible
*   Thai support toggle

Middle:

*   hint card optional with possible pattern  
    Example: “I want \_\_\_.”

Bottom:

*   large mic response area

### Footer

*   replay question
*   hint button
*   mic
*   skip optional

### States

*   with hint
*   no hint
*   after response shows recognition + feedback

* * *

3.10H Dialogue turn step
------------------------

### Body

Top:

*   context badge: “At Home” / “Food” / “Shopping”
*   progress indicator: Turn 2 of 4

Middle:

*   speech bubbles
    *   app turn left aligned
    *   learner turn right aligned after response
*   current prompt bubble highlighted

Bottom of body:

*   response input area with mic
*   optional answer hint chips

### Footer

*   replay prompt
*   slow audio
*   mic
*   continue after success

### States

*   awaiting reply
*   processing reply
*   accepted response
*   retry with hint

* * *

3.10I Step feedback state
-------------------------

Can appear inline or as bottom sheet after speaking.

### Components

*   score ring or simple badge
*   brief message:
    *   Good job
    *   Try final sound again
    *   Stress the first part
*   buttons:
    *   Try Again
    *   Continue

* * *

3.11 Lesson pause / exit modal
==============================

Purpose
-------

Prevent accidental loss

Layout
------

Centered modal:

*   title: Leave lesson?
*   message: Your progress will be saved.  
    Buttons:
*   Continue lesson
*   Leave lesson

* * *

3.12 Lesson completion screen
=============================

Purpose
-------

Celebrate completion and summarize learning

Layout
------

### Header

None or simple title

### Body

Centered celebration block:

*   checkmark / badge
*   “Lesson Complete”

Below:

*   words learned count
*   sentence practiced count
*   speaking score summary
*   difficult sounds flagged if any

Secondary card:

*   next recommended action
    *   Start next lesson
    *   Review hard words
    *   Practice sound W

### Footer

*   primary button: Next Lesson
*   secondary button: Review Hard Words
*   text button: Back to Home

* * *

#### Category cards

*   Final consonants

Each card contains:

*   icon
*   short subtitle
*   mastery progress

Lower section:

*   recommended practice today

### Bottom navigation

Visible

Actions
-------

Tap category → Sound Category List

3.14 Sound category list screen
===============================

Purpose
-------

Show sounds within category

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   category title

### Body

Grid or list of sound cards:

*   /a/
*   /e/
*   /r/
*   /l/
*   /v/
*   /w/  
    Each card includes:
*   sound symbol
*   example word
*   difficulty indicator
*   completion ring

Actions
-------

Tap sound → Sound Detail / Practice

* * *

3.15 Sound detail / practice screen
===================================

Purpose
-------

Deep practice on one sound

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   sound symbol title

### Body

Top section:

*   large sound symbol
*   description in Thai
*   mouth position hint
*   play normal / slow

Middle section:

*   example words list
*   each row:
    *   word
    *   Thai meaning
    *   play button

Lower section:

*   speak the sound
*   big mic button
*   “practice 5 times” counter

Bottom section:

*   button: Compare with similar sound

### Footer

*   previous sound
*   next sound

* * *

3.16 Minimal pairs screen
=========================

Purpose
-------

Compare commonly confused sounds

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   title: “Compare Sounds”

### Body

Top:

*   pair title, e.g. R / L

Middle:  
For one pair item:

*   word A card: light
*   word B card: right  
    Each card:
*   play audio
*   Thai meaning
*   small image optional

Below:

*   question: “What did you hear?”
*   two large answer buttons

Then:

*   “Say word A”
*   mic button
*   “Say word B”
*   mic button

### Footer

*   next pair
*   finish

### States

*   listening mode
*   choose mode
*   repeat mode

* * *

3.19 Word detail screen
=======================

Purpose
-------

Single word learning and review

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   favorite icon

### Body

Top:

*   image
*   English word large
*   Thai meaning
*   pronunciation hint
*   syllable split
*   optional IPA hidden by default under “More”

Middle:  
Audio controls:

*   play
*   slow
*   repeat loop

Next:  
Example sentence card:

*   sentence
*   Thai translation
*   play sentence

Next:  
Practice box:

*   big mic button
*   playback learner recording
*   pronunciation feedback

Bottom:  
Related words or minimal pair links

### Footer

*   previous word
*   next word

3.20 Vocabulary review screen
=============================

Purpose
-------

Run word review session

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   title: “Review Words”
*   progress count 3/10

### Body

Changes by review type:

#### Mode 1: Audio to meaning

*   play audio
*   4 answer cards

#### Mode 2: Picture to word

*   large image
*   4 answer cards

#### Mode 3: Word to speech

*   show word
*   mic button

#### Mode 4: Sentence fill

*   “I want \_\_\_.”
*   choose correct word

### Footer

*   continue
*   optional skip

### End state

*   review result screen with correct count

* * *

3.21 Sentence pattern hub
=========================

Purpose
-------

Organize sentence structures

Layout
------

### Header

*   title: “Sentences”

### Body

Pattern cards:

*   This is \_\_\_.
*   I want \_\_\_.
*   I need \_\_\_.
*   Where is \_\_\_?
*   Do you want \_\_\_?
*   Can you help me?

Each card includes:

*   example
*   mastery percentage
*   current difficulty

### Actions

Tap pattern → Sentence Pattern Detail

* * *

*   I want rice.

Lower:  
Substitution chips:

*   water
*   tea
*   rice
*   help

Practice area:

*   prompt to say new sentence

Bottom:  
Mini dialogue using pattern

*   start drill
*   back to patterns

3.31 Partner practice session screen

Show prompts for two-person practice

------

*   back
*   session title

    *   Partner
    *   Learner

Middle:  
Prompt cards one at a time  
Example:

*   Partner says: “What do you want?”

Optional:

*   play model audio
*   show Thai help
*   reveal answer button

3.33 Review session screen
==========================

Purpose
-------

Run mixed spaced repetition session

Layout
------

### Header

*   back
*   title
*   progress count

### Body

Dynamic by content type:

*   word card
*   sound compare
*   sentence speaking
*   dialogue recall

Bottom area:

*   confidence buttons optional:
    *   Easy
    *   Okay
    *   Hard

### Footer

*   continue

### Behavior

Used to reschedule item difficulty

* * *

5\. Reusable components spec
============================

* * *

5.1 Audio control cluster
=========================

Components:

*   play/replay button
*   slow audio button
*   loop button optional
*   progress waveform optional

Used on:

*   lesson steps
*   words
*   sentences
*   sounds
*   dialogues

* * *

5.2 Mic button
==============

States:

*   idle
*   recording
*   processing
*   disabled

Visual rules:

*   always prominent
*   label changes with state
*   error state shows retry

* * *

5.3 Word card component
=======================

Fields:

*   image
*   English
*   Thai
*   pronunciation hint
*   mastery chip
*   speaker button

* * *

5.4 Sentence card component
===========================

Fields:

*   English sentence
*   Thai translation
*   audio button
*   optional pattern badge

* * *

5.5 Progress bar
================

Used on:

*   lesson progress
*   review progress
*   course completion

Types:

*   thin top bar
*   segmented bar
*   circular ring for summary only

* * *

5.6 Feedback chip
=================

Examples:

*   Good
*   Try Again
*   Slow Down
*   Last Sound Missing

Used after speaking attempts

* * *

5.7 Hint chip
=============

Example:

*   I want \_\_\_.
*   Say: “Yes, please.”

Tap reveals or inserts hint

* * *

6\. Screen state matrix
=======================

Key screen states to design for
-------------------------------

### Lesson Player

*   idle
*   audio playing
*   awaiting speech
*   recording
*   processing
*   success
*   retry
*   network fail

### Dialogue Practice

*   prompt playing
*   waiting
*   recognized correct
*   recognized close
*   failed and hint shown

### Review Session

*   unanswered
*   correct
*   incorrect
*   completed

### Home

*   new learner
*   active learner
*   no review due
*   offline mode

* * *

7\. Navigation summary
======================

Main learner flow
-----------------

Splash → Language → Onboarding → Account Setup → Level Check → Home → Lesson Intro → Lesson Player → Lesson Completion → Home

Practice flow
-------------

Home / Sounds / Speak / Review → selected practice mode → session → result → next recommendation

Admin flow
----------

Admin Login → Dashboard → Content area → Edit/Create → Preview → Publish

* * *

8\. Responsive behavior notes
=============================

Small phones
------------

*   stack cards vertically
*   keep footer buttons fixed
*   collapse secondary metadata
*   use bottom sheets for hints/settings

Larger phones
-------------

*   more breathing room
*   dialogue bubbles may widen
*   keep single-column learner layout

Tablet
------

*   learner mode still mostly single column
*   admin mode can support side panels

* * *

9\. Design handoff notes
========================

For the designer, each of these wireframes should be turned into:

*   low-fidelity grayscale frames first
*   clickable prototype for core flow
*   then visual system and component library

The most important prototype to build first is:

1.  Home
2.  Lesson Intro
3.  Lesson Player
4.  Dialogue Practice
5.  Pronunciation Feedback
6.  Lesson Completion
7.  Review Session

That is the critical user journey.

The best next deliverable is a **clickable screen flow map with component inventory**, or a **Figma-ready frame list with exact frame names and hierarchy**.

## Prompt:
07/04/2026, 21:16:52

Continue

## Response:
07/04/2026, 21:16:53

I’m extending the wireframe package into production-ready handoff detail: named frames, screen states, and exact component inventory so it can be mapped directly into Figma and tickets.

> Thought for 5s

Below is the continuation: a **Figma-ready frame list, screen-flow map, component inventory, interaction rules, and handoff structure**.

This turns the wireframe spec into something a designer and frontend team can execute directly.

10\. Figma-ready frame list
===========================

Use a naming system that stays stable.

Recommended page structure in Figma
-----------------------------------

### Page 1: Foundations

*   Colors
*   Typography
*   Spacing
*   Icons
*   Grid
*   Tokens

### Page 2: Components

*   Buttons
*   Inputs
*   Cards
*   Audio controls
*   Mic states
*   Feedback chips
*   Bottom navigation
*   Modals
*   Empty states

### Page 3: Learner App — Core Flow

*   Splash
*   Onboarding
*   Home
*   Lesson
*   Completion

### Page 4: Learner App — Practice

*   Sounds
*   Words
*   Sentences
*   Dialogues
*   Review

### Page 5: Learner App — Settings/Profile

*   Profile
*   Settings
*   Downloads
*   Help

### Page 6: Learner App — States

*   Loading
*   Empty
*   Error
*   Permission blocked
*   Offline

### Page 7: Admin Web

*   Dashboard
*   Lists
*   Editors
*   Preview

* * *

Exact frame naming convention
-----------------------------

Format:

**\[Platform\] / \[Area\] / \[Screen\] / \[Variant\]**

Examples:

*   Mobile / Onboarding / Language Select / Default
*   Mobile / Home / Dashboard / Returning User
*   Mobile / Lesson / Player / Speak Sentence - Recording
*   Mobile / Dialogue / Practice / Retry With Hint
*   Web / Admin / Lesson Editor / Default

* * *

11\. Screen flow map
====================

11.1 Primary learner flow
-------------------------

### First-time user

Splash  
→ Language Select  
→ Welcome Carousel  
→ Account Setup  
→ Level Check  
→ Start Result  
→ Home  
→ Lesson Intro  
→ Lesson Player  
→ Lesson Completion  
→ Home

### Returning user

Splash  
→ Home  
→ Continue Lesson or Review  
→ Completion / Results  
→ Home

* * *

11.2 Lesson flow
----------------

Lesson Intro  
→ Step 1 Listen  
→ Step 2 Repeat  
→ Step 3 Syllables  
→ Step 4 Word Cards  
→ Step 5 Sentence Practice  
→ Step 6 Guided Question  
→ Step 7 Mini Dialogue  
→ Lesson Completion

Exit points:

*   pause modal
*   network retry
*   save progress and leave

* * *

11.3 Practice flow
------------------

Home / Sounds tab / Review tab / Speak tab  
→ choose practice area  
→ choose item or recommended pack  
→ practice session  
→ result / recommendation  
→ next practice or home

* * *

11.4 Review flow
----------------

Home → Review Due Today  
or  
Bottom Nav → Review  
→ Quick Review  
→ mixed exercises  
→ result  
→ recommended hard-item review

* * *

11.5 Dialogue flow
------------------

Speak Hub  
→ Dialogues Hub  
→ Scenario Intro  
→ Dialogue Practice  
→ Dialogue Result  
→ Suggested Next Dialogue

* * *

12\. Component inventory
========================

This is the component library the designer should build first.

* * *

12.1 Buttons
============

Primary button
--------------

Usage:

*   Continue
*   Start Lesson
*   Save
*   Next

States:

*   default
*   pressed
*   disabled
*   loading

Specs:

*   full-width on mobile
*   high contrast
*   single label line

Secondary button
----------------

Usage:

*   Back
*   Skip
*   Review Hard Words

States:

*   default
*   pressed
*   disabled

Text button
-----------

Usage:

*   Skip
*   Change later
*   Reveal answer

Icon button
-----------

Usage:

*   back
*   close
*   settings
*   favorite
*   replay

Sizes:

*   small
*   medium
*   large

* * *

12.2 Audio controls
===================

Speaker button
--------------

Usage:

*   play normal audio

States:

*   idle
*   playing
*   disabled

Slow audio button
-----------------

Usage:

*   replay slow version

States:

*   idle
*   playing

Loop audio button
-----------------

Usage:

*   repeated pronunciation practice

Optional in MVP

Audio cluster component
-----------------------

Includes:

*   play
*   slow
*   optional loop
*   optional waveform

* * *

12.3 Mic components
===================

Primary mic button
------------------

Usage:

*   record response

States:

*   idle
*   recording
*   processing
*   success
*   retry

Requirements:

*   large tap target
*   status label underneath

Recording waveform panel
------------------------

Usage:

*   show active input

States:

*   animated during recording
*   static during playback

Voice result panel
------------------

Contains:

*   transcript
*   pronunciation status
*   retry button
*   continue button

* * *

12.4 Cards
==========

Lesson card
-----------

Fields:

*   lesson number
*   title
*   duration
*   progress
*   CTA

Review card
-----------

Fields:

*   type
*   due count
*   short action text

Word card
---------

Fields:

*   image
*   word
*   Thai meaning
*   pronunciation hint
*   mastery

Sentence card
-------------

Fields:

*   sentence
*   Thai translation
*   audio
*   pattern badge optional

Dialogue scenario card
----------------------

Fields:

*   title
*   context
*   turns count
*   difficulty
*   completion

Progress stat card
------------------

Fields:

*   metric
*   value
*   sublabel

* * *

12.5 Inputs
===========

Text input
----------

Usage:

*   name
*   search
*   admin editors

Select / dropdown
-----------------

Usage:

*   language
*   category
*   lesson assignment
*   admin filters

Chip selector
-------------

Usage:

*   goals
*   pace
*   categories
*   filters

Time picker
-----------

Usage:

*   reminders

* * *

12.6 Feedback components
========================

Feedback chip
-------------

Labels:

*   Good
*   Great
*   Try Again
*   Slow Down
*   Last Sound Missing

Feedback card
-------------

Contains:

*   short title
*   one or two suggestions
*   optional replay button

Success banner
--------------

Usage:

*   lesson complete
*   review complete
*   dialogue done

Error banner
------------

Usage:

*   no internet
*   speech failed
*   permission blocked

Bottom tab bar

Tabs:

*   Home

*   Sounds
*   Speak

States:

*   active
*   inactive
*   notification badge optional

Top app bar

Variants:

*   title only
*   back + title
*   title + action
*   close + progress

Progress bar
------------

Variants:

*   thin lesson progress
*   segmented review progress
*   circular completion ring

13\. Component rules
====================

Spacing system
--------------

Use a simple scale:

*   4
*   8
*   12
*   16
*   24
*   32

Corner radius
-------------

Recommended:

*   cards: medium
*   buttons: medium/large
*   chips: pill
*   modals: large

Touch targets
-------------

Minimum:

*   44x44

Mic button:

*   larger than all other controls

Hierarchy
---------

Most prominent element by screen:

*   lesson screen: mic or next action
*   home: today’s lesson
*   review: current question
*   dialogue: current prompt + mic

* * *

14\. Detailed interaction spec by screen
========================================

* * *

14.1 Home interactions
======================

### Today’s lesson card

Tap → open Lesson Intro or resume Lesson Player

### Review card

Tap → open Review Hub or direct session if only one due type

### Recent word chip

Tap → open Word Detail

### Streak badge

Tap → open Progress

* * *

14.2 Lesson player interactions
===============================

### Replay audio

Tap replay button  
Result:

*   replay current prompt
*   restart animation if any

### Slow audio

Tap slow audio  
Result:

*   play slowed version or generated slower version

### Mic record

Tap mic  
Result:

*   begin recording
*   show recording state
*   after stop, send for processing

### Next

Enabled after:

*   listen step completed
*   answer chosen
*   speech attempt made or skipped

### Hint

Available on certain steps only

### Exit

Tap close  
→ Pause modal

* * *

14.3 Review interactions
========================

### Correct answer

*   highlight correct
*   short positive feedback
*   auto-enable continue

### Wrong answer

*   show correct answer
*   optionally replay audio
*   reschedule item harder

### Confidence choice

At end of some review items:

*   Easy
*   Okay
*   Hard

Used to adjust queue timing

* * *

14.4 Dialogue interactions
==========================

### App turn

Auto-plays on entry unless autoplay off

### Learner response

Tap mic to answer

### Accepted response

*   transcript shown in learner bubble
*   continue enabled

### Near match

*   feedback shown
*   allow retry without penalty or minor penalty

### Failed response

*   hint chip appears
*   replay prompt available
*   can retry or skip

* * *

15\. State design details
=========================

* * *

15.1 Loading states
===================

Full screen loading
-------------------

Use for:

*   splash
*   initial content load
*   admin dashboard initial fetch

Inline loading
--------------

Use for:

*   word list fetch
*   review generation
*   analytics chart loading

Speech processing loading
-------------------------

Use for:

*   pronunciation scoring
*   transcript result  
    Display:
*   short status text
*   subtle animation

* * *

15.2 Empty states
=================

Each empty state should include:

*   icon/illustration
*   one-line status
*   one useful CTA

Examples:

*   No review due → Practice Sounds
*   No favorites → Explore Words
*   No downloads → Download Week 1 Pack

* * *

15.3 Error states
=================

Recoverable error
-----------------

*   message
*   retry
*   continue later

Blocking error
--------------

*   message
*   action required

Example:  
mic permission denied:

*   Open Settings
*   Learn Without Voice

* * *

15.4 Offline states
===================

App offline banner
------------------

Sticky top or inline:

*   “You’re offline. Some voice features may not work.”

Offline lesson mode
-------------------

If lesson assets cached:

*   continue with local content
*   disable online scoring or defer upload

* * *

16\. Content display rules
==========================

English text
------------

Primary, larger

Thai meaning
------------

Secondary, smaller, beneath English

Pronunciation hint
------------------

Tertiary, small, lighter emphasis

IPA
---

Hidden by default, optional “More” or advanced mode

Images
------

Use when concrete noun/action benefits from visual aid

Audio
-----

Always easy to access

* * *

17\. Typography hierarchy recommendation
========================================

Not branding design, just structure.

Level 1
-------

Screen titles

Level 2
-------

Card titles  
Lesson words  
Main prompts

Level 3
-------

Thai translations  
Supporting labels  
Explanations

Level 4
-------

Metadata  
Progress labels  
System notes

Rule:  
Do not crowd screens with many text sizes. Keep to 4 levels maximum.

* * *

18\. Accessibility and usability requirements
=============================================

Learner-side
------------

*   support large text mode
*   strong contrast
*   captions available
*   simple language
*   no dense menus
*   audio alternatives for all key learning content
*   visible progress so user knows where they are

Speech UX
---------

*   always allow retry
*   never punish one failed pronunciation harshly
*   keep feedback short and actionable

* * *

19\. Handoff checklist for design
=================================

The designer should deliver:

Low-fidelity
------------

*   full flow wireframes
*   all key state variants
*   navigation map

Mid-fidelity
------------

*   componentized screens
*   reusable cards/buttons/modals
*   spacing consistency

High-fidelity
-------------

*   visual system
*   iconography
*   illustration direction
*   motion notes
*   clickable prototype

Prototype priority
------------------

Build clickable prototype for:

*   onboarding
*   home
*   lesson
*   speaking feedback
*   dialogue
*   review

* * *

20\. Engineering handoff checklist
==================================

Each screen should include:

*   frame name
*   route name
*   state variants
*   data dependencies
*   user actions
*   validation rules
*   empty/error handling
*   analytics events

Example for one screen:

**Screen:** Mobile / Lesson / Player / Speak Sentence  
**Route:** `/lesson/:lessonId/step/:stepId`  
**Data needed:** lesson step, sentence, audio URLs, hint, pass rule  
**Actions:** replay, slow audio, record, retry, continue  
**Events:** lesson\_step\_viewed, audio\_replayed, speech\_started, speech\_scored, lesson\_step\_completed

* * *

23\. Motion notes
=================

Keep motion minimal and functional.

Recommended motions
-------------------

*   progress bar advancing
*   subtle audio pulse on play
*   mic pulse when recording
*   card lift on correct answer
*   success check animation on completion

Avoid
-----

*   overly playful motion
*   long transitions
*   distracting background animations

* * *

24\. Final recommended build order for screens
==============================================

For fastest real product progress, design and implement in this order:

Batch 1
-------

*   Splash
*   Language Select
*   Onboarding
*   Home
*   Lesson Intro
*   Lesson Player
*   Lesson Completion

Batch 2
-------

*   Sounds Hub
*   Sound Detail
*   Word Detail
*   Word Review
*   Review Hub

Batch 3
-------

*   Speak Hub
*   Dialogue Intro
*   Dialogue Practice
*   Pronunciation Feedback
*   Progress

Batch 4
-------

*   Profile
*   Settings
*   Downloads
*   Help

Batch 5
-------

*   Admin Dashboard
*   Lesson Editor
*   Word Editor
*   Dialogue Editor
*   Analytics

* * *

25\. Most important final note
==============================

The app should feel like:

*   one clear action at a time
*   listen first
*   speak safely
*   retry without stress
*   always understand what to do next

That matters more than visual complexity.

The best next step is a **developer-ready component spec with props and state definitions**, or a **Supabase SQL schema with real table definitions and indexes**.

## Prompt:
07/04/2026, 21:59:30

 API contract in detail

## Response:
07/04/2026, 21:59:33

I’m converting the product structure into a detailed API contract: endpoints, request/response schemas, auth model, idempotency, pagination, and error handling so backend and mobile can build against the same interface.

> Thought for 6s

Below is a **detailed API contract** for the app.

It is designed for:

*   mobile client developers
*   backend developers
*   admin web developers
*   QA
*   product

This contract assumes:

*   REST JSON API
*   token-based auth
*   media files stored separately
*   speech processing handled by API-backed services

I will define:

1.  API conventions
2.  Authentication
3.  Learner endpoints
4.  Content endpoints
5.  Progress endpoints
6.  Review endpoints
7.  Speech endpoints
8.  Dialogue endpoints
9.  Admin endpoints
10.  Webhooks/internal jobs
11.  Error model
12.  Pagination/filtering
13.  Example payloads
14.  Recommended versioning rules

* * *

1\. API conventions
===================

Base URL
--------

```
https://api.yourapp.com/v1
```

Content type
------------

Requests:

```
Content-Type: application/json
```

Responses:

```
Content-Type: application/json
```

For file upload:

```
Content-Type: multipart/form-data
```

Authentication
--------------

Protected endpoints require:

```
Authorization: Bearer <access_token>
```

Time format
-----------

Use ISO 8601 UTC:

```
"2026-04-07T09:30:00Z"
```

ID format
---------

Use UUIDs or stable string IDs.

Examples:

```
"id": "9d0f4d1b-84ef-4d92-8e20-0a5a4a3f3e75"
```

or

```
"id": "lesson_009"
```

Be consistent across the system.

Response envelope
-----------------

Use a consistent response structure.

### Success

```
{
  "data": {},
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

### Failure

```
{
  "data": null,
  "meta": {},
  "error": {
    "code": "INVALID_REQUEST",
    "message": "The request body is invalid.",
    "details": [
      {
        "field": "name",
        "issue": "required"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

* * *

2\. Authentication API
======================

* * *

2.1 Create guest session
------------------------

### POST `/auth/guest`

Creates an anonymous learner session.

### Request

```
{
  "device_id": "device_abc123",
  "interface_language": "th",
  "app_version": "1.0.0"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "user": {
      "id": "user_001",
      "is_guest": true,
      "display_name": "Learner",
      "interface_language": "th"
    },
    "access_token": "jwt_access_token",
    "refresh_token": "jwt_refresh_token",
    "expires_in": 3600
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

2.2 Register account
--------------------

### POST `/auth/signup`

### Request

```
{
  "email": "user@example.com",
  "password": "StrongPassword123!",
  "display_name": "Mali",
  "interface_language": "th"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "user": {
      "id": "user_001",
      "email": "user@example.com",
      "display_name": "Mali",
      "is_guest": false
    },
    "access_token": "jwt_access_token",
    "refresh_token": "jwt_refresh_token",
    "expires_in": 3600
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

2.3 Login
---------

### POST `/auth/login`

### Request

```
{
  "email": "user@example.com",
  "password": "StrongPassword123!"
}
```

### Response

Same shape as signup.

* * *

2.4 Refresh token
-----------------

### POST `/auth/refresh`

### Request

```
{
  "refresh_token": "jwt_refresh_token"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "access_token": "new_access_token",
    "refresh_token": "new_refresh_token",
    "expires_in": 3600
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

2.5 Convert guest to registered account
---------------------------------------

### POST `/auth/upgrade-guest`

### Request

```
{
  "email": "user@example.com",
  "password": "StrongPassword123!"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "user": {
      "id": "user_001",
      "email": "user@example.com",
      "is_guest": false
    }
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

2.6 Logout
----------

### POST `/auth/logout`

### Request

```
{
  "refresh_token": "jwt_refresh_token"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "logged_out": true
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

3\. Learner profile and settings API
====================================

3.1 Get current user
--------------------

### GET `/me`

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "id": "user_001",
    "display_name": "Mali",
    "email": "user@example.com",
    "native_language": "th",
    "interface_language": "th",
    "learning_goal": "daily_life",
    "current_level_id": "level_0",
    "current_lesson_id": "lesson_001",
    "is_guest": false,
    "created_at": "2026-04-07T09:30:00Z"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

-----------------------

### PATCH `/me`

### Request

```
{
  "display_name": "Mali",
  "learning_goal": "home_conversation",
  "native_language": "th"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "id": "user_001",
    "display_name": "Mali",
    "learning_goal": "home_conversation",
    "native_language": "th"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

3.3 Get settings
----------------

### GET `/me/settings`

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "interface_language": "th",
    "thai_translation_enabled": true,
    "bilingual_mode": true,
    "preferred_voice_gender": "female",
    "audio_speed_default": "normal",
    "subtitles_enabled": true,
    "notifications_enabled": true,
    "daily_reminder_time": "19:00:00",
    "save_recordings": true,
    "strict_answer_mode": false
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

3.4 Update settings
-------------------

### PATCH `/me/settings`

### Request

```
{
  "preferred_voice_gender": "female",
  "audio_speed_default": "slow",
  "daily_reminder_time": "20:00:00",
  "thai_translation_enabled": true
}
```

### Response

  "data": {
    "updated": true
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null

  "learning_goal": "daily_life",
  "pace": "slow"
}
```

### Response

  "data": {
    "saved": true
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null

---------------------------

### POST `/onboarding/placement-answer`

{
  "onboarding_session_id": "onb_001",

  "answer": {
    "type": "choice",
    "value": "do_not_understand"
  }
}
```

### Response

  "data": {
    "accepted": true,
    "next_question_id": "placement_q2"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}

  "onboarding_session_id": "onb_001"

    "recommended_lesson_id": "lesson_001",

  "error": null

      "description": "Pronunciation-first English course",
      "source_language": "th",
      "target_language": "en",
      "version": 1,
      "is_published": true

  "error": null

    "description": "Pronunciation-first English course",
    "levels": [
      {
        "id": "level_0",

      }
    ]

            "id": "module_week_1",

                  }

    "subtitle": "Practice W sound",
    "estimated_minutes": 12,
    "lesson_type": "standard",
    "sound_focus": {

        "english_text": "water",

        "id": "word_yes",
        "english_text": "yes",
        "thai_text": "ใช่"

    "target_sentences": [

7\. Lesson progress API
=======================

* * *

7.1 Start lesson
----------------

### POST `/lessons/{lesson_id}/start`

### Request

```
{
  "source": "home"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "lesson_progress_id": "lp_001",
    "status": "in_progress",
    "started_at": "2026-04-07T09:35:00Z"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

7.2 Save step progress
----------------------

### POST `/lessons/{lesson_id}/steps/{step_id}/progress`

### Request

```
{
  "status": "completed",
  "attempts": 1,
  "time_spent_seconds": 28,
  "score": {
    "overall": 78,
    "pronunciation": 75
  },
  "response_summary": {
    "selected_answer": "น้ำ",
    "recognized_text": null
  }
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "saved": true,
    "lesson_completion_percent": 33
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

7.3 Get lesson progress
-----------------------

### GET `/lessons/{lesson_id}/progress`

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "lesson_id": "lesson_009",
    "status": "in_progress",
    "current_step_id": "step_003",
    "completion_percent": 33,
    "retry_count": 2,
    "time_spent_seconds": 184
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

7.4 Complete lesson
-------------------

### POST `/lessons/{lesson_id}/complete`

### Request

```
{
  "final_score": {
    "overall": 81,
    "pronunciation": 74,
    "comprehension": 89
  }
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "lesson_id": "lesson_009",
    "status": "completed",
    "completed_at": "2026-04-07T09:48:00Z",
    "awards": [
      {
        "code": "lesson_complete",
        "title": "Lesson Complete"
      }
    ],
    "recommended_next_actions": [
      {
        "type": "lesson",
        "target_id": "lesson_010",
        "title": "Next Lesson"
      },
      {
        "type": "review",
        "target_id": "review_words_hard",
        "title": "Review Hard Words"
      }
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

  "speaking_score": 74,
  "listening_score": 82,
  "mark_hard": false
}

{

  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}

{
  "data": {
    "due_today": {
      "words": 8,
      "sounds": 2,
      "sentences": 3,
      "dialogues": 1
    },
    "hard_items": {
      "words": 4,
      "sounds": 2
    },
    "recommended_mode": "quick_review"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

9.2 Get review queue
--------------------

### GET `/review/queue`

### Query params

*   `mode=quick_review`
*   `content_type=word`
*   `limit=10`

### Response

```
{
  "data": [
    {
      "review_id": "rq_001",
      "content_type": "word",
      "content_id": "word_water",
      "reason": "due_review",
      "priority": 10,
      "exercise_type": "audio_to_meaning"
    },
    {
      "review_id": "rq_002",
      "content_type": "sound",
      "content_id": "sound_r",
      "reason": "low_accuracy",
      "priority": 9,
      "exercise_type": "minimal_pair"
    }
  ],
  "meta": {
    "next_cursor": "cursor_002"
  },
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

------------------------

### POST `/review/{review_id}/complete`

### Request

```
{
  "result": "correct",
  "confidence": "okay",
  "time_spent_seconds": 11,
  "score": 78
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "completed": true,
    "next_review_at": "2026-04-09T09:00:00Z"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}

* * *

10\. Speech and pronunciation API
=================================

This is critical for the app.

* * *

10.1 Create upload URL for recording
------------------------------------

### POST `/speech/uploads`

Returns pre-signed upload target or upload token.

### Request

```
{
  "content_type": "audio/m4a",
  "context": {
    "lesson_id": "lesson_009",
    "step_id": "step_004"
  }
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "upload_id": "upl_001",
    "upload_url": "https://storage.yourapp.com/presigned-url",
    "asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_001.m4a",
    "expires_at": "2026-04-07T10:00:00Z"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

10.2 Submit audio for transcription
-----------------------------------

### POST `/speech/transcribe`

### Request

```
{
  "audio_asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_001.m4a",
  "language": "en",
  "context": {
    "type": "lesson_step",
    "lesson_id": "lesson_009",
    "step_id": "step_004"
  }
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "transcript_text": "I want water",
    "confidence": 0.91,
    "words": [
      {
        "text": "I",
        "start_ms": 0,
        "end_ms": 120
      },
      {
        "text": "want",
        "start_ms": 130,
        "end_ms": 420
      },
      {
        "text": "water",
        "start_ms": 430,
        "end_ms": 900
      }
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

10.3 Score pronunciation of a word
----------------------------------

### POST `/speech/pronunciation/word`

### Request

```
{
  "audio_asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_001.m4a",
  "target_word_id": "word_water",
  "target_text": "water"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "overall_score": 71,
    "phoneme_score": 68,
    "stress_score": 74,
    "final_sound_score": 80,
    "feedback": [
      {
        "code": "STRESS_FIRST_SYLLABLE",
        "message": "Stress the first part: WA-ter."
      }
    ],
    "phoneme_feedback": [
      {
        "part": "wa",
        "score": 76
      },
      {
        "part": "ter",
        "score": 63
      }
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

10.4 Score pronunciation of a sentence
--------------------------------------

### POST `/speech/pronunciation/sentence`

### Request

```
{
  "audio_asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_001.m4a",
  "target_sentence_id": "sentence_i_want_water",
  "target_text": "I want water."
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "overall_score": 76,
    "word_scores": [
      {
        "word": "I",
        "score": 88
      },
      {
        "word": "want",
        "score": 80
      },
      {
        "word": "water",
        "score": 63
      }
    ],
    "stress_score": 72,
    "fluency_score": 70,
    "feedback": [
      {
        "code": "TRY_LAST_WORD_AGAIN",
        "message": "Try the last word again."
      }
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

10.5 Score sound production
---------------------------

### POST `/speech/pronunciation/sound`

### Request

```
{
  "audio_asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_001.m4a",
  "target_sound_id": "sound_r"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "overall_score": 54,
    "feedback": [
      {
        "code": "TRY_TONGUE_POSITION",
        "message": "Lift your tongue slightly and try again."
      }
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

10.6 Save speaking attempt
--------------------------

### POST `/speech/attempts`

### Request

```
{
  "lesson_step_id": "step_004",
  "word_id": "word_water",
  "sentence_id": null,
  "dialogue_id": null,
  "audio_asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_001.m4a",
  "transcript_text": "water",
  "recognition_confidence": 0.93,
  "pronunciation_score": 71,
  "feedback_text": "Stress the first part: WA-ter."
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "attempt_id": "attempt_001"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

11\. Dialogue API
=================

* * *

11.1 List dialogues
-------------------

### GET `/dialogues`

### Query params

*   `context=food`
*   `level_id=level_0`
*   `mode=guided`

### Response

```
{
  "data": [
    {
      "id": "dialogue_food_001",
      "title": "Ordering Water",
      "context": "food",
      "mode": "guided",
      "turn_count": 4,
      "difficulty": "beginner"
    }
  ],
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

11.2 Get dialogue detail
------------------------

### GET `/dialogues/{dialogue_id}`

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "id": "dialogue_food_001",
    "title": "Ordering Water",
    "description": "Practice asking for a drink",
    "context": "food",
    "mode": "guided",
    "target_phrases": [
      "I want water.",
      "Yes, please."
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

11.3 Get dialogue turns
-----------------------

### GET `/dialogues/{dialogue_id}/turns`

### Response

```
{
  "data": [
    {
      "turn_id": "turn_001",
      "speaker": "app",
      "text": "Do you want water?",
      "thai_text": "คุณต้องการน้ำไหม",
      "audio_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/audio/dialogues/do_you_want_water.mp3"
    },
    {
      "turn_id": "turn_002",
      "speaker": "learner",
      "expected_answers": [
        "Yes, please.",
        "Yes please."
      ],
      "validation_type": "exact_or_normalized",
      "hint_text": "Say: Yes, please."
    }
  ],
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

11.4 Start dialogue session
---------------------------

### POST `/dialogues/{dialogue_id}/start`

### Request

```
{
  "mode": "guided"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "dialogue_session_id": "ds_001",
    "current_turn_id": "turn_001",
    "status": "in_progress"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

11.5 Submit dialogue response
-----------------------------

### POST `/dialogue-sessions/{session_id}/respond`

### Request

```
{
  "turn_id": "turn_002",
  "audio_asset_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/user-audio/upl_002.m4a",
  "transcript_text": "Yes, please."
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "accepted": true,
    "score": 88,
    "feedback": "Good job.",
    "next_turn": {
      "turn_id": "turn_003",
      "speaker": "app",
      "text": "Here you are.",
      "thai_text": "นี่ค่ะ/ครับ",
      "audio_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/audio/dialogues/here_you_are.mp3"
    }
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

11.6 Retry dialogue response
----------------------------

### Request

```
{
  "turn_id": "turn_002"
}
```

```
{
  "data": {
    "retry_allowed": true,
    "hint_text": "Say: Yes, please.",
    "replay_audio_url": "https://cdn.yourapp.com/audio/dialogues/do_you_want_water.mp3"
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

16\. Admin API
==============

Protected by admin role.

* * *

16.1 List lessons
-----------------

### GET `/admin/lessons`

### Query params

*   `search=water`
*   `unit_id=unit_week_2`
*   `published=true`

### Response

```
{
  "data": [
    {
      "id": "lesson_009",
      "title": "Water and Yes",
      "unit_id": "unit_week_2",
      "estimated_minutes": 12,
      "is_published": true,
      "updated_at": "2026-04-07T08:00:00Z"
    }
  ],
  "meta": {
    "next_cursor": null
  },
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

16.2 Create lesson
------------------

### POST `/admin/lessons`

### Request

```
{
  "unit_id": "unit_week_2",
  "lesson_order": 9,
  "title": "Water and Yes",
  "subtitle": "Practice W sound",
  "estimated_minutes": 12,
  "lesson_type": "standard",
  "sound_focus_id": "sound_w"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "id": "lesson_009",
    "created": true
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

16.3 Update lesson
------------------

### PATCH `/admin/lessons/{lesson_id}`

### Request

```
{
  "title": "Water and Yes",
  "estimated_minutes": 13,
  "is_published": true
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "updated": true
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

--------------------

### POST `/admin/lessons/{lesson_id}/steps`

### Request

```
{
  "step_order": 1,
  "step_type": "audio_listen",
  "instruction_en": "Listen",
  "instruction_th": "ฟัง",
  "payload": {
    "sound_id": "sound_w",
    "audio_asset_id": "asset_audio_w"
  },
  "passing_rule": {
    "auto_pass_after_play": true
  }
}
```

```
{
  "data": {
    "id": "step_001",
    "created": true

  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}

  "error": null

{
  "data": {
    "daily_active_users": 1420,
    "lesson_completion_rate": 0.61,
    "avg_pronunciation_score": 67.4,
    "top_failed_sounds": [

        "sound_id": "sound_r",
        "failure_rate": 0.48
      }
    ]
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

18\. Error model
================

Use stable error codes.

Standard error object
---------------------

```
{
  "error": {
    "code": "INVALID_REQUEST",
    "message": "The request body is invalid.",
    "details": [
      {
        "field": "english_text",
        "issue": "required"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Common error codes
------------------

*   `INVALID_REQUEST`
*   `UNAUTHORIZED`
*   `FORBIDDEN`
*   `NOT_FOUND`
*   `CONFLICT`
*   `RATE_LIMITED`
*   `VALIDATION_FAILED`
*   `MIC_PERMISSION_REQUIRED`
*   `SPEECH_PROCESSING_FAILED`
*   `UPLOAD_EXPIRED`
*   `LESSON_LOCKED`
*   `STEP_NOT_AVAILABLE`
*   `DIALOGUE_RESPONSE_INVALID`
*   `INTERNAL_ERROR`

Example
-------

```
{
  "data": null,
  "meta": {},
  "error": {
    "code": "LESSON_LOCKED",
    "message": "This lesson is locked until the previous lesson is completed.",
    "details": []
  }
}
```

* * *

19\. HTTP status code rules
===========================

Use
---

*   `200 OK` for successful GET/PATCH/POST where no new resource location needed
*   `201 Created` for new admin resource creation
*   `400 Bad Request` for malformed input
*   `401 Unauthorized` for missing/invalid token
*   `403 Forbidden` for role restrictions
*   `404 Not Found`
*   `409 Conflict`
*   `422 Unprocessable Entity` for validation failures
*   `429 Too Many Requests`
*   `500 Internal Server Error`

* * *

20\. Pagination, filtering, sorting
===================================

For list endpoints, use cursor pagination.

Query params
------------

*   `limit=20`
*   `cursor=abc123`
*   `sort=updated_at`
*   `order=desc`

Response meta
-------------

```
{
  "meta": {
    "next_cursor": "cursor_002",
    "limit": 20
  }
}
```

Filter examples
---------------

```
GET /admin/lessons?unit_id=unit_week_2&published=true&limit=20
GET /words?category=food&favorites=true
GET /dialogues?context=shopping&level_id=level_0
```

* * *

21\. Idempotency rules
======================

For operations that may be retried by mobile clients, support idempotency.

Use header:

```
Idempotency-Key: <uuid>
```

Recommended for:

*   `/lessons/{lesson_id}/start`
*   `/lessons/{lesson_id}/complete`
*   `/speech/attempts`
*   `/dialogues/{dialogue_id}/start`
*   `/dialogue-sessions/{session_id}/respond`

* * *

22\. Field enum recommendations
===============================

interface\_language
-------------------

*   `th`
*   `en`
*   `bilingual`

learning\_goal
--------------

*   `daily_life`
*   `home_conversation`
*   `travel`
*   `start_from_zero`

lesson\_type
------------

*   `standard`
*   `review`
*   `sound_focus`
*   `dialogue_focus`

step\_type
----------

*   `audio_listen`
*   `audio_repeat`
*   `syllable_drill`
*   `word_flashcard`
*   `image_match`
*   `listen_choose`
*   `speak_word`
*   `speak_sentence`
*   `speak_answer`
*   `dialogue_turn`
*   `review_quiz`

dialogue mode
-------------

*   `guided`
*   `repeat`
*   `open`

review content\_type
--------------------

*   `word`
*   `sound`
*   `sentence`
*   `dialogue`

result values
-------------

*   `correct`
*   `incorrect`
*   `partial`
*   `skipped`

* * *

23\. Mobile caching rules
=========================

Good candidates for caching:

*   course map
*   lesson detail
*   lesson steps
*   words
*   sounds
*   dialogues metadata
*   download manifests

Should not be blindly cached long-term:

*   review queue
*   home recommendations
*   progress
*   speaking scores

* * *

24\. Security and privacy requirements in API
=============================================

Protected data
--------------

*   user profile
*   speech recordings
*   transcripts
*   progress history
*   admin content actions

Requirements
------------

*   signed URLs expire quickly
*   audio upload auth required
*   recordings deletable by user
*   minimal data retention policy
*   transcripts only accessible to owner/admin where appropriate

Delete user recordings
----------------------

### DELETE `/me/recordings`

### Request

```
{
  "scope": "all"
}
```

### Response

```
{
  "data": {
    "deleted_count": 24
  },
  "meta": {},
  "error": null
}
```

* * *

25\. Recommended backend split
==============================

For cleaner implementation, separate these services logically:

Auth service
------------

*   login
*   signup
*   tokens

Content service
---------------

*   courses
*   lessons
*   words
*   sounds
*   dialogues

Progress service
----------------

*   lessons progress
*   review queue
*   mastery tracking

Speech service
--------------

*   upload
*   transcription
*   pronunciation scoring

Admin CMS service
-----------------

*   create/edit/publish content

Analytics service
-----------------

*   event ingestion
*   reporting

They can still sit behind one API gateway.

* * *

26\. Recommended OpenAPI grouping
=================================

If documented in OpenAPI/Swagger, group tags like this:

*   Auth
*   Me
*   Onboarding
*   Courses
*   Lessons
*   Words
*   Sentences
*   Sounds
*   MinimalPairs
*   Home
*   Progress
*   Review
*   Speech
*   Dialogues
*   Downloads
*   Notifications
*   Achievements
*   AdminLessons
*   AdminWords
*   AdminSentences
*   AdminSounds
*   AdminDialogues
*   AdminAssets
*   AdminAnalytics

* * *

27\. Recommended next step
==========================

The most useful next artifact would be either:

*   a full **OpenAPI 3.1 YAML spec**
*   a **Supabase/Postgres SQL schema**
*   a **Firebase/Firestore API mapping**
*   a **backend implementation task breakdown**

The strongest follow-up is the **OpenAPI 3.1 spec**, because engineering can generate clients and mocks from it.

## Prompt:
07/04/2026, 22:09:03

full OpenAPI 3.1 YAML spec

## Response:
07/04/2026, 22:09:04

I’m packaging the contract as a real OpenAPI 3.1 document so it can be imported into Swagger, Stoplight, or codegen tools directly. I’ll include reusable schemas, security, pagination, learner endpoints, speech endpoints, and admin endpoints.

Thought for 9s

Analyzed

```
from pathlib import Path

yaml_content = r'''openapi: 3.1.0
info:
  title: Easy English Thai API
  version: 1.0.0
  summary: Pronunciation-first beginner English learning API for Thai speakers
  description: |
    REST API for a mobile-first English learning app focused on Thai-speaking beginners.
    Supports onboarding, lessons, words, sounds, reviews, pronunciation scoring,
    dialogues, downloads, notifications, analytics, and admin CMS operations.
  contact:
    name: API Team
servers:
  - url: https://api.yourapp.com/v1
    description: Production
  - url: https://staging-api.yourapp.com/v1
    description: Staging

jsonSchemaDialect: https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema

tags:
  - name: Auth
  - name: Me
  - name: Onboarding
  - name: Courses
  - name: Lessons
  - name: Words
  - name: Sentences
  - name: Sounds
  - name: MinimalPairs
  - name: Home
  - name: Progress
  - name: Review
  - name: Speech
  - name: Dialogues
  - name: Downloads
  - name: Notifications
  - name: Achievements
  - name: Search
  - name: Analytics
  - name: AdminLessons
  - name: AdminWords
  - name: AdminSentences
  - name: AdminSounds
  - name: AdminDialogues
  - name: AdminAssets
  - name: AdminQA
  - name: AdminAnalytics

security:
  - bearerAuth: []

paths:
  /auth/guest:
    post:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Create guest session
      operationId: createGuestSession
      security: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/CreateGuestSessionRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Guest session created
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'
        '422':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ValidationError'

  /auth/signup:
    post:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Register account
      operationId: signup
      security: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/SignupRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Account created
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'
        '409':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ConflictError'
        '422':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ValidationError'

  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Login
      operationId: login
      security: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login successful
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'
        '401':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/UnauthorizedError'

  /auth/refresh:
    post:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Refresh access token
      operationId: refreshToken
      security: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/RefreshTokenRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token refreshed
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/RefreshTokenResponse'
        '401':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/UnauthorizedError'

  /auth/upgrade-guest:
    post:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Convert guest account into registered account
      operationId: upgradeGuest
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/UpgradeGuestRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Guest upgraded
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/UpgradeGuestResponse'
        '409':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ConflictError'

  /auth/logout:
    post:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Logout
      operationId: logout
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LogoutRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Logout completed
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/LogoutResponse'

  /me:
    get:
      tags: [Me]
      summary: Get current user profile
      operationId: getMe
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Current user
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/GetMeResponse'
    patch:
      tags: [Me]
      summary: Update current user profile
      operationId: updateMe
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/UpdateMeRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: User updated
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/GetMeResponse'
        '422':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ValidationError'

  /me/settings:
    get:
      tags: [Me]
      summary: Get learner settings
      operationId: getMySettings
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Settings
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/GetSettingsResponse'
    patch:
      tags: [Me]
      summary: Update learner settings
      operationId: updateMySettings
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/UpdateSettingsRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Settings updated
          content:

          $ref: '#/components/responses/ForbiddenError'
    post:
      tags: [AdminLessons]

        - bearerAuth: []

        required: true

          description: Lesson created

            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AdminCreateEntityResponse'

  securitySchemes:

      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT

  parameters:

      required: false

      required: true

      in: query

        type: string
        enum: [en, th]

      name: published
      in: query

        type: boolean

      name: category
      in: query
      schema:
        type: string

      name: difficulty
      in: query

        type: string
        enum: [beginner, intermediate, advanced]

      name: search
      in: query

        type: string

      in: query
      required: true

        type: string

        example: word,sentence,dialogue

        type: integer

        type: string
        format: date

  responses:

    post:
      tags: [Notifications]
      summary: Review due notification event webhook
      operationId: reviewDueWebhook
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/ReviewDueEvent'
            examples:
              default:
                $ref: '#/components/examples/ReviewDueEventExample'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Webhook accepted
'''
    text = text.replace('\ncomponents:\n', webhooks + '\ncomponents:\n', 1)

# Add examples component section if absent
if '\n  examples:\n' not in text:
    insertion = r'''
  examples:
    AuthResponseExample:
      value:
        data:
          user:
            id: user_001
            email: user@example.com
            display_name: Mali
            native_language: th
            interface_language: th

          refresh_token: jwt_refresh_token

        meta: {}
        error: null

          words: 8
          sounds: 2
          sentences: 3
          dialogues: 1
'''
    text = text.replace('\n  schemas:\n', insertion + '\n  schemas:\n', 1)

# Add event schemas if absent
if 'LessonCompletedEvent:' not in text:
    event_schemas = r'''
    EventBase:
      type: object
      properties:
        event_id:
          type: string
        event_type:
          type: string
        occurred_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        user_id:
          type: string
      required: [event_id, event_type, occurred_at, user_id]

    LessonCompletedEvent:
      allOf:
        - $ref: '#/components/schemas/EventBase'
        - type: object
          properties:
            lesson_id:
              type: string
            score:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/ScoreBundle'
          required: [lesson_id, score]

    PronunciationScoredEvent:
      allOf:
        - $ref: '#/components/schemas/EventBase'
        - type: object
          properties:
            content_type:
              type: string
              enum: [sound, word, sentence]
            content_id:
              type: string
            attempt_id:
              type: string
            overall_score:
              type: number
            feedback_codes:
              type: array
              items:
                type: string
          required: [content_type, content_id, attempt_id, overall_score, feedback_codes]

    ReviewDueEvent:
      allOf:
        - $ref: '#/components/schemas/EventBase'
        - type: object
          properties:
            due_counts:
              type: object
              properties:
                words:
                  type: integer
                sounds:
                  type: integer
                sentences:
                  type: integer
                dialogues:
                  type: integer
              required: [words, sounds, sentences, dialogues]
          required: [due_counts]
'''
    # append before end of schemas by inserting before AdminLessonListItem schema
    text = text.replace('\n    AdminLessonListItem:\n', event_schemas + '\n    AdminLessonListItem:\n', 1)

# Add examples refs to key operations if missing
replacements = {
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/AuthResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetHomeResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetHomeResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetHomeResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetLessonResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetLessonResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetLessonResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetLessonStepsResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetLessonStepsResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetLessonStepsResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetWordResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetWordResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetWordResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetSentenceResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetSentenceResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetSentenceResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetSoundResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetSoundResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetSoundResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetReviewQueueResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/GetReviewQueueResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/GetReviewQueueResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/TranscribeSpeechResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/TranscribeSpeechResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/TranscribeSpeechResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/ScoreWordPronunciationResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/ScoreWordPronunciationResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/ScoreWordPronunciationResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/StartDialogueSessionResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/StartDialogueSessionResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/StartDialogueSessionResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/RespondDialogueSessionResponse'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/RespondDialogueSessionResponse'\n                examples:\n                  default:\n                    $ref: '#/components/examples/RespondDialogueSessionResponseExample'\n",
    "$ref: '#/components/schemas/AdminCreateLessonRequest'\n": "$ref: '#/components/schemas/AdminCreateLessonRequest'\n            examples:\n              default:\n                $ref: '#/components/examples/AdminCreateLessonRequestExample'\n",
}
for old, new in replacements.items():
    text = text.replace(old, new, 1 if "AdminCreateLessonRequest" in old else text.count(old))

# Basic "validated/refined" additions: external docs and common operation response descriptions remain.
out = Path('/mnt/data/easy-english-thai-openapi-3.1-refined.yaml')
out.write_text(text, encoding='utf-8')
print(f"Wrote {out} ({out.stat().st_size} bytes)")
