```
from pathlib import Path

sql = r"""
-- Easy English Thai
-- Postgres / Supabase SQL schema
-- Version: 1.0.0
-- Matches the OpenAPI 3.1 contract artifacts generated previously.

-- Recommended extensions
create extension if not exists pgcrypto;

-- =========================================================
-- ENUMS
-- =========================================================

do $$
begin
  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'interface_language_enum') then
    create type interface_language_enum as enum ('th', 'en', 'bilingual');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'voice_speed_enum') then
    create type voice_speed_enum as enum ('slow', 'normal');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'learning_goal_enum') then
    create type learning_goal_enum as enum ('daily_life', 'home_conversation', 'travel', 'start_from_zero');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'difficulty_level_enum') then
    create type difficulty_level_enum as enum ('beginner', 'intermediate', 'advanced');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'lesson_type_enum') then
    create type lesson_type_enum as enum ('standard', 'review', 'sound_focus', 'dialogue_focus');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'step_type_enum') then
    create type step_type_enum as enum (
      'audio_listen',
      'audio_repeat',
      'syllable_drill',
      'word_flashcard',
      'image_match',
      'listen_choose',
      'speak_word',
      'speak_sentence',
      'speak_answer',
      'dialogue_turn',
      'review_quiz'
    );
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'dialogue_mode_enum') then
    create type dialogue_mode_enum as enum ('guided', 'repeat', 'open');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'review_content_type_enum') then
    create type review_content_type_enum as enum ('word', 'sound', 'sentence', 'dialogue');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'review_result_enum') then
    create type review_result_enum as enum ('correct', 'incorrect', 'partial', 'skipped');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'lesson_progress_status_enum') then
    create type lesson_progress_status_enum as enum ('not_started', 'in_progress', 'completed');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'speaker_enum') then
    create type speaker_enum as enum ('app', 'learner');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'voice_gender_enum') then
    create type voice_gender_enum as enum ('male', 'female');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'platform_enum') then
    create type platform_enum as enum ('ios', 'android');
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'asset_type_enum') then
    create type asset_type_enum as enum (
      'image',
      'audio_normal',
      'audio_slow',
      'mouth_diagram',
      'icon',
      'user_recording',
      'other'
    );
  end if;

  if not exists (select 1 from pg_type where typname = 'analytics_event_name_enum') then
    create type analytics_event_name_enum as enum (
      'onboarding_started',
      'language_selected',
      'onboarding_completed',
      'level_check_started',
      'level_check_completed',
      'home_viewed',
      'today_lesson_tapped',
      'review_tapped',
      'sound_practice_tapped',
      'lesson_started',
      'lesson_step_viewed',
      'audio_played',
      'audio_slow_played',
      'mic_started',
      'mic_completed',
      'speech_scored',
      'hint_opened',
      'lesson_completed',
      'review_started',
      'review_item_answered',
      'review_item_marked_hard',
      'review_completed',
      'dialogue_started',
      'dialogue_turn_attempted',
      'dialogue_turn_passed',
      'dialogue_turn_failed',
      'dialogue_completed',
      'setting_changed',
      'reminder_set',
      'download_started',
      'download_removed'
    );
  end if;
end$$;

-- =========================================================
-- GENERIC UPDATED_AT TRIGGER
-- =========================================================

create or replace function set_updated_at()
returns trigger
language plpgsql
as $$
begin
  new.updated_at = now();
  return new;
end;
$$;

-- =========================================================
-- CORE IDENTITY / USER TABLES
-- =========================================================

create table if not exists users (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  auth_user_id uuid unique, -- can map to auth.users.id in Supabase
  email text unique,
  phone text unique,
  display_name text not null,
  native_language text,
  interface_language interface_language_enum not null default 'th',
  learning_goal learning_goal_enum not null default 'start_from_zero',
  current_level_id uuid,
  current_lesson_id uuid,
  is_guest boolean not null default true,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  constraint users_email_or_guest_chk check (
    is_guest = true or email is not null or phone is not null
  )
);

create trigger users_set_updated_at
before update on users
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists user_settings (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id uuid not null unique references users(id) on delete cascade,
  interface_language interface_language_enum not null default 'th',
  thai_translation_enabled boolean not null default true,
  bilingual_mode boolean not null default true,
  preferred_voice_gender voice_gender_enum not null default 'female',
  audio_speed_default voice_speed_enum not null default 'normal',
  subtitles_enabled boolean not null default true,
  notifications_enabled boolean not null default true,
  daily_reminder_time time,
  save_recordings boolean not null default true,
  strict_answer_mode boolean not null default false,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now()
);

create trigger user_settings_set_updated_at
before update on user_settings
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists device_tokens (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id uuid not null references users(id) on delete cascade,
  platform platform_enum not null,
  device_token text not null,
  device_id text not null,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (platform, device_token),
  unique (user_id, device_id)
);

-- =========================================================
-- COURSE / CURRICULUM STRUCTURE
-- =========================================================

create table if not exists courses (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  stable_key text unique,
  title text not null,
  description text not null,
  source_language text not null,
  target_language text not null,
  version integer not null default 1,
  is_published boolean not null default false,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now()
);

create trigger courses_set_updated_at
before update on courses
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists levels (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  course_id uuid not null references courses(id) on delete cascade,
  stable_key text unique,
  level_order integer not null,
  title text not null,
  description text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (course_id, level_order)
);

create trigger levels_set_updated_at
before update on levels
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists modules (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  level_id uuid not null references levels(id) on delete cascade,
  stable_key text unique,
  module_order integer not null,
  title text not null,
  description text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (level_id, module_order)
);

create trigger modules_set_updated_at
before update on modules
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists units (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  module_id uuid not null references modules(id) on delete cascade,
  stable_key text unique,
  unit_order integer not null,
  title text not null,
  description text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (module_id, unit_order)
);

create trigger units_set_updated_at
before update on units
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists sounds (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  stable_key text unique,
  sound_code text not null,
  display_symbol text not null,
  title text not null,
  description_th text not null,
  mouth_hint text,
  category text not null,
  thai_difficulty_flag boolean not null default false,
  audio_demo_normal_url text,
  audio_demo_slow_url text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (sound_code)
);

create trigger sounds_set_updated_at
before update on sounds
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists lessons (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  stable_key text unique,
  unit_id uuid not null references units(id) on delete cascade,
  lesson_order integer not null,
  title text not null,
  subtitle text,
  estimated_minutes integer not null check (estimated_minutes > 0),
  lesson_type lesson_type_enum not null default 'standard',
  sound_focus_id uuid references sounds(id) on delete set null,
  is_review_lesson boolean not null default false,
  is_published boolean not null default false,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (unit_id, lesson_order)
);

create trigger lessons_set_updated_at
before update on lessons
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

create table if not exists lesson_steps (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  stable_key text unique,
  lesson_id uuid not null references lessons(id) on delete cascade,
  step_order integer not null,
  step_type step_type_enum not null,
  title text,
  instruction_en text not null,
  instruction_th text not null,
  payload_json jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  passing_rule_json jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  unique (lesson_id, step_order)
);

create trigger lesson_steps_set_updated_at
before update on lesson_steps
for each row execute function set_updated_at();

-- =========================================================

alter table users
  drop constraint if exists users_current_level_id_fkey,
  add constraint users_current_level_id_fkey
    foreign key (current_level_id) references levels(id) on delete set null;

  drop constraint if exists users_current_lesson_id_fkey,
  add constraint users_current_lesson_id_fkey
    foreign key (current_lesson_id) references lessons(id) on delete set null;

create index if not exists idx_dialogues_level on dialogues(level_id);
create index if not exists idx_dialogues_context on dialogues(context_type);
create index if not exists idx_dialogues_published on dialogues(is_published);
create index if not exists idx_dialogue_turns_dialogue_order on dialogue_turns(dialogue_id, turn_order);

create index if not exists idx_onboarding_sessions_user on onboarding_sessions(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_onboarding_answers_session on onboarding_answers(onboarding_session_id);

create index if not exists idx_user_lesson_progress_user on user_lesson_progress(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_user_lesson_progress_lesson on user_lesson_progress(lesson_id);
create index if not exists idx_user_lesson_step_progress_user_lesson on user_lesson_step_progress(user_id, lesson_id);

create index if not exists idx_user_word_progress_user on user_word_progress(user_id);

create index if not exists idx_user_word_progress_hard on user_word_progress(user_id, is_hard_word);

create index if not exists idx_user_sound_progress_user on user_sound_progress(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_user_sound_progress_next_review on user_sound_progress(next_review_at);

create index if not exists idx_user_sentence_progress_user on user_sentence_progress(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_user_sentence_progress_next_review on user_sentence_progress(next_review_at);

create index if not exists idx_dialogue_sessions_user on dialogue_sessions(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_dialogue_sessions_dialogue on dialogue_sessions(dialogue_id);

create index if not exists idx_user_speaking_attempts_user on user_speaking_attempts(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_user_speaking_attempts_created on user_speaking_attempts(created_at);

create index if not exists idx_review_queue_due on review_queue(user_id, due_at);
create index if not exists idx_review_queue_content on review_queue(user_id, content_type, content_id);

create index if not exists idx_analytics_events_user on analytics_events(user_id);
create index if not exists idx_analytics_events_name on analytics_events(event_name);
create index if not exists idx_analytics_events_time on analytics_events(event_time);

create index if not exists idx_content_qa_issues_status on content_qa_issues(status);
create index if not exists idx_content_qa_issues_type on content_qa_issues(content_type, issue_type);

-- =========================================================
-- VIEW HELPERS
-- =========================================================

create or replace view v_course_map as
select
  c.id as course_id,
  c.title as course_title,
  l.id as level_id,
  l.level_order,
  l.title as level_title,
  m.id as module_id,
  m.module_order,
  m.title as module_title,
  u.id as unit_id,
  u.unit_order,
  u.title as unit_title,
  les.id as lesson_id,
  les.lesson_order,
  les.title as lesson_title,
  les.is_published
from courses c
join levels l on l.course_id = c.id
join modules m on m.level_id = l.id
join units u on u.module_id = m.id
join lessons les on les.unit_id = u.id;

create or replace view v_review_due_counts as
select
  user_id,
  content_type,
  count(*) filter (where completed_at is null and due_at <= now()) as due_count
from review_queue
group by user_id, content_type;

-- =========================================================
-- OPTIONAL: ROW LEVEL SECURITY STARTER NOTES
-- =========================================================
-- For Supabase, you would typically:
--   alter table <table_name> enable row level security;
-- and then add policies such as:
--   users can select/update their own rows
--   users can insert/select/update their own progress rows
--   only admins can access admin tables
--
-- Those policies are intentionally omitted here because exact auth strategy
-- depends on whether you map users.auth_user_id to auth.uid() directly.

"""
path = Path('/mnt/data/easy-english-thai-supabase-postgres-schema.sql')
path.write_text(sql, encoding='utf-8')
print(f"Wrote {path} ({path.stat().st_size} bytes)")
```

```
from pathlib import Path

sql = r"""
-- Easy English Thai
-- Supabase Row Level Security (RLS) policies
-- Assumes:
--   1) public.users.auth_user_id maps to auth.uid()
--   2) admin users are listed in public.admin_users via public.users.id
--   3) content tables are readable by authenticated users only when published
--   4) learner-owned tables are readable/writable only by the owning learner

-- =========================================================
-- HELPER FUNCTIONS
-- =========================================================

create or replace function public.current_app_user_id()
returns uuid
language sql
stable
as $$
  select u.id
  from public.users u
  where u.auth_user_id = auth.uid()
  limit 1
$$;

create or replace function public.is_admin_user()
returns boolean
language sql
stable
as $$
  select exists (
    select 1
    from public.admin_users au
    join public.users u on u.id = au.user_id
    where u.auth_user_id = auth.uid()
  )
$$;

-- =========================================================
-- ENABLE RLS
-- =========================================================

alter table public.users enable row level security;
alter table public.user_settings enable row level security;
alter table public.device_tokens enable row level security;

alter table public.courses enable row level security;
alter table public.levels enable row level security;
alter table public.modules enable row level security;
alter table public.units enable row level security;
alter table public.lessons enable row level security;
alter table public.lesson_steps enable row level security;

alter table public.assets enable row level security;
alter table public.sentence_patterns enable row level security;
alter table public.words enable row level security;
alter table public.sentences enable row level security;
alter table public.sentence_words enable row level security;
alter table public.lesson_words enable row level security;
alter table public.lesson_sentences enable row level security;

-- ADMIN WRITE ACCESS TO CONTENT TABLES
-- =========================================================

do $$
declare
  tbl text;
  tables text[] := array[
    'courses','levels','modules','units','lessons','lesson_steps',
    'assets','sentence_patterns','words','sentences','sentence_words',
    'lesson_words','lesson_sentences','word_sounds','minimal_pair_groups',
    'minimal_pair_items','dialogues','dialogue_turns','download_packs','download_pack_files'
  ];
begin
  foreach tbl in array tables
  loop
    execute format('drop policy if exists %I on public.%I', tbl || '_admin_all', tbl);
    execute format(
      'create policy %I on public.%I for all to authenticated using (public.is_admin_user()) with check (public.is_admin_user())',
      tbl || '_admin_all',
      tbl
    );
  end loop;
end$$;

-- =========================================================
-- OPTIONAL STORAGE NOTES
-- =========================================================
-- If using Supabase Storage for learner audio:
--   - create a private bucket for user recordings
--   - allow upload/read/delete only when the object path includes auth.uid()
-- Example path pattern:
--   recordings/<auth.uid()>/<uuid>.m4a
--
-- Storage policies are not included here because they depend on bucket names.

"""
path = Path('/mnt/data/easy-english-thai-supabase-rls-policies.sql')
path.write_text(sql, encoding='utf-8')
print(f"Wrote {path} ({path.stat().st_size} bytes)")
```

```
from pathlib import Path

sql = r"""
-- Easy English Thai
-- Supabase Storage bucket layout and storage policies
-- Assumptions:
--   1) auth.uid() is available
--   2) public.users.auth_user_id maps to auth.uid()
--   3) public.is_admin_user() function exists from the RLS policy file
--   4) public.current_app_user_id() exists, though storage policies mostly use auth.uid()

-- =========================================================
-- BUCKET LAYOUT
-- =========================================================
-- Public content buckets:
--   lesson-audio       -> published lesson audio (normal/slow)
--   lesson-images      -> word images, diagrams, icons
--   downloadable-packs -> downloadable audio/content pack files
--
-- Private bucket:
--   user-recordings    -> learner speech recordings
--
-- Suggested object key patterns:
--
-- lesson-audio:
--   courses/<course_key>/lessons/<lesson_key>/<filename>.mp3
--   sounds/<sound_key>/<variant>.mp3
--   dialogues/<dialogue_key>/<turn_order>.mp3
--
-- lesson-images:
--   words/<word_key>/<filename>.png
--   sounds/<sound_key>/<filename>.png
--   icons/<filename>.svg
--
-- downloadable-packs:
--   packs/<pack_key>/<filename>.zip
--   manifests/<pack_key>.json
--
-- user-recordings:
--   users/<auth.uid()>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<uuid>.m4a

-- =========================================================
-- CREATE BUCKETS
-- =========================================================

insert into storage.buckets (id, name, public)
values
  ('lesson-audio', 'lesson-audio', true),
  ('lesson-images', 'lesson-images', true),
  ('downloadable-packs', 'downloadable-packs', true),
  ('user-recordings', 'user-recordings', false)
on conflict (id) do update
set public = excluded.public;

-- =========================================================
-- HELPER FUNCTIONS FOR STORAGE
-- =========================================================

create or replace function public.storage_foldername(name text)
returns text[]
language sql
immutable
as $$
  select string_to_array(name, '/')
$$;

create or replace function public.storage_user_owns_path(name text)
returns boolean
language sql
stable
as $$
  select
    coalesce((public.storage_foldername(name))[1], '') = 'users'
    and coalesce((public.storage_foldername(name))[2], '') = auth.uid()::text
$$;

-- =========================================================
-- CLEAN SLATE: DROP EXISTING POLICIES IF PRESENT
-- =========================================================

drop policy if exists "lesson-audio public read" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "lesson-images public read" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "downloadable-packs public read" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "admins manage public media" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "users read own recordings" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "users upload own recordings" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "users update own recordings" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "users delete own recordings" on storage.objects;
drop policy if exists "admins manage user recordings" on storage.objects;

-- =========================================================
-- PUBLIC READ ACCESS FOR PUBLISHED APP MEDIA
-- =========================================================
-- Since these buckets are public, direct file serving is allowed.
-- These policies protect object table access through SQL/API.

create policy "lesson-audio public read"
on storage.objects
for select
to public
using (bucket_id = 'lesson-audio');

create policy "lesson-images public read"
on storage.objects
for select
to public
using (bucket_id = 'lesson-images');

create policy "downloadable-packs public read"
on storage.objects
for select
to public
using (bucket_id = 'downloadable-packs');

-- =========================================================
-- ADMIN MANAGEMENT OF PUBLIC CONTENT BUCKETS
-- =========================================================

create policy "admins manage public media"
on storage.objects
for all
to authenticated
using (
  public.is_admin_user()
  and bucket_id in ('lesson-audio', 'lesson-images', 'downloadable-packs')
)
with check (
  public.is_admin_user()
  and bucket_id in ('lesson-audio', 'lesson-images', 'downloadable-packs')
);

-- =========================================================
-- PRIVATE USER RECORDINGS
-- =========================================================
-- Users can only manage objects in:
--   user-recordings / users / <auth.uid()> / ...

create policy "users read own recordings"
on storage.objects
for select
to authenticated
using (
  bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
  and public.storage_user_owns_path(name)
);

create policy "users upload own recordings"
on storage.objects
for insert
to authenticated
with check (
  bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
  and public.storage_user_owns_path(name)
);

create policy "users update own recordings"
on storage.objects
for update
to authenticated
using (
  bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
  and public.storage_user_owns_path(name)
)
with check (
  bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
  and public.storage_user_owns_path(name)
);

create policy "users delete own recordings"
on storage.objects
for delete
to authenticated
using (
  bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
  and public.storage_user_owns_path(name)
);

-- =========================================================
-- ADMIN ACCESS TO PRIVATE RECORDINGS
-- =========================================================

create policy "admins manage user recordings"
on storage.objects
for all
to authenticated
using (
  public.is_admin_user()
  and bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
)
with check (
  public.is_admin_user()
  and bucket_id = 'user-recordings'
);

-- =========================================================
-- OPTIONAL TIGHTENING NOTES
-- =========================================================
-- If you want to force file types by path or extension, add checks like:
--   lower(right(name, 4)) = '.mp3'
--   lower(right(name, 4)) = '.m4a'
--   lower(right(name, 4)) = '.png'
--
-- Example:
--   and lower(right(name, 4)) = '.m4a'
--
-- You can also separate dialogue audio and lesson audio into more buckets if
-- you want stricter lifecycle management.

-- =========================================================
-- RECOMMENDED STORAGE CONVENTIONS
-- =========================================================
-- lesson-audio:
--   sounds/sound_w/normal.mp3
--   sounds/sound_w/slow.mp3
--   lessons/lesson_009/step_001.mp3
--   dialogues/dialogue_food_001/turn_001.mp3
--
-- lesson-images:
--   words/word_water/main.png
--   sounds/sound_th/mouth.png
--   ui/icons/mic.svg
--
-- downloadable-packs:
--   packs/week_1/week_1_audio.zip
--   manifests/week_1.json
--
-- user-recordings:
--   users/<auth.uid()>/2026/04/<uuid>.m4a

"""
path = Path('/mnt/data/easy-english-thai-supabase-storage-policies.sql')
path.write_text(sql, encoding='utf-8')
print(f"Wrote {path} ({path.stat().st_size} bytes)")
```

```
from pathlib import Path
import json

# Build a practical starter seed SQL pack.
lines = []
lines.append("-- Easy English Thai")
lines.append("-- Seed data pack")
lines.append("-- Bootstraps course, first 12 weeks, core sounds, starter words, sentence patterns, and starter dialogues")
lines.append("begin;")
lines.append("")

# Course
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- COURSE")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("""
insert into courses (stable_key, title, description, source_language, target_language, version, is_published)
values
  ('course_en_for_thai_beginner', 'Beginner English for Thai Speakers', 'Pronunciation-first beginner English course for Thai-speaking learners', 'th', 'en', 1, true)
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    description = excluded.description,
    source_language = excluded.source_language,
    target_language = excluded.target_language,
    version = excluded.version,
    is_published = excluded.is_published;
""")

# Level
lines.append("""
insert into levels (course_id, stable_key, level_order, title, description)
select c.id, 'level_0', 1, 'Absolute Beginner', 'Starts from zero with sounds, syllables, small words, and short sentences'
from courses c
where c.stable_key = 'course_en_for_thai_beginner'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    description = excluded.description,
    level_order = excluded.level_order;
""")

# Modules/weeks + units
for week in range(1, 13):
    lines.append(f"""
insert into modules (level_id, stable_key, module_order, title, description)
select l.id, 'module_week_{week}', {week}, 'Week {week}', 'Week {week} learning module'
from levels l
where l.stable_key = 'level_0'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    description = excluded.description,
    module_order = excluded.module_order;
""")
    lines.append(f"""
insert into units (module_id, stable_key, unit_order, title, description)
select m.id, 'unit_week_{week}', 1, 'Week {week} Unit', 'Primary unit for week {week}'
from modules m
where m.stable_key = 'module_week_{week}'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    description = excluded.description,
    unit_order = excluded.unit_order;
""")

# Sounds
sounds = [
    ("sound_a_short","a","A","Short A","เสียง a สั้น เช่น cat","สระ",True),
    ("sound_e_short","e","E","Short E","เสียง e สั้น เช่น bed","สระ",True),
    ("sound_i_short","i","I","Short I","เสียง i สั้น เช่น sit","สระ",True),
    ("sound_o_short","o","O","Short O","เสียง o สั้น เช่น hot","สระ",True),
    ("sound_u_short","u","U","Short U","เสียง u สั้น เช่น cup","สระ",True),
    ("sound_b","b","B","B sound","เสียง บ","consonant",False),
    ("sound_p","p","P","P sound","เสียง พ/ป ลมชัด","consonant",True),
    ("sound_m","m","M","M sound","เสียง ม","consonant",False),
    ("sound_t","t","T","T sound","เสียง ท/ต","consonant",True),
    ("sound_d","d","D","D sound","เสียง ด","consonant",True),
    ("sound_n","n","N","N sound","เสียง น","consonant",False),
    ("sound_k","k","K","K sound","เสียง ค/ก ลมชัด","consonant",True),
    ("sound_g","g","G","G sound","เสียง ก","consonant",True),
    ("sound_s","s","S","S sound","เสียง ส","consonant",False),
    ("sound_z","z","Z","Z sound","เสียง ซ/สั่น","consonant",True),
    ("sound_f","f","F","F sound","เสียง ฟ ใช้ฟันแตะริมฝีปาก","consonant",True),
    ("sound_v","v","V","V sound","เสียง วี/ฟันแตะริมฝีปากมีเสียง","consonant",True),
    ("sound_w","w","W","W sound","เสียง ว","consonant",True),
    ("sound_l","l","L","L sound","เสียง ล","consonant",True),
    ("sound_r","r","R","R sound","เสียง ร อังกฤษ","consonant",True),
    ("sound_sh","sh","SH","SH sound","เสียง ช/ช์ เช่น she","consonant",True),
    ("sound_ch","ch","CH","CH sound","เสียง ช เช่น chair","consonant",True),
    ("sound_j","j","J","J sound","เสียง จ เช่น job","consonant",True),
    ("sound_th_unvoiced","th","TH","TH sound (thin)","เสียง th เช่น thin","consonant",True),
    ("sound_th_voiced","th_voiced","TH","TH sound (this)","เสียง th เช่น this","consonant",True),
    ("sound_ng","ng","NG","NG final sound","เสียง ง ท้ายคำ","consonant",True),
]
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- SOUNDS")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for stable_key, sound_code, display_symbol, title, desc_th, category, thai_diff in sounds:
    lines.append(f"""
insert into sounds (stable_key, sound_code, display_symbol, title, description_th, category, thai_difficulty_flag)
values ('{stable_key}', '{sound_code}', '{display_symbol}', '{title}', '{desc_th}', '{category}', {'true' if thai_diff else 'false'})
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set sound_code = excluded.sound_code,
    display_symbol = excluded.display_symbol,
    title = excluded.title,
    description_th = excluded.description_th,
    category = excluded.category,
    thai_difficulty_flag = excluded.thai_difficulty_flag;
""")

# Sentence patterns
patterns = [
    ("pattern_this_is_blank","This is ___.","นี่คือ___","ใช้ชี้สิ่งของหรือคน","beginner"),
    ("pattern_that_is_blank","That is ___.","นั่นคือ___","ใช้ชี้สิ่งที่อยู่ไกล","beginner"),
    ("pattern_it_is_blank","It is ___.","มันคือ/มันเป็น___","ใช้บอกลักษณะหรือสถานะ","beginner"),
    ("pattern_i_am_blank","I am ___.","ฉันเป็น/ฉันรู้สึก___","ใช้แนะนำตัวหรือบอกความรู้สึก","beginner"),
    ("pattern_i_want_blank","I want ___.","ฉันต้องการ___","ใช้บอกสิ่งที่ต้องการ","beginner"),
    ("pattern_i_need_blank","I need ___.","ฉันต้องการ___","ใช้บอกความจำเป็น","beginner"),
    ("pattern_i_like_blank","I like ___.","ฉันชอบ___","ใช้บอกสิ่งที่ชอบ","beginner"),
    ("pattern_where_is_blank","Where is ___?","___อยู่ที่ไหน","ใช้ถามหาของหรือสถานที่","beginner"),
    ("pattern_do_you_want_blank","Do you want ___?","คุณต้องการ___ไหม","ใช้ถามความต้องการ","beginner"),
    ("pattern_can_you_help_me","Can you help me?","คุณช่วยฉันได้ไหม","ใช้ขอความช่วยเหลือ","beginner"),
]
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- SENTENCE PATTERNS")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for sk, pt, th, expl, diff in patterns:
    lines.append(f"""
insert into sentence_patterns (stable_key, pattern_text, pattern_text_th, explanation_th, difficulty_level)
values ('{sk}', '{pt.replace("'", "''")}', '{th}', '{expl}', '{diff}')
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set pattern_text = excluded.pattern_text,
    pattern_text_th = excluded.pattern_text_th,
    explanation_th = excluded.explanation_th,
    difficulty_level = excluded.difficulty_level;
""")

for sk, en, th, syll, pos, cat, diff in words:
    syll_arr = "{" + ",".join(syll) + "}"
    lines.append(f"""
insert into words (stable_key, english_text, thai_text, syllable_split, part_of_speech, category, difficulty_level)
values ('{sk}', '{en.replace("'", "''")}', '{th}', '{syll_arr}', '{pos}', '{cat}', '{diff}')
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set english_text = excluded.english_text,
    thai_text = excluded.thai_text,
    syllable_split = excluded.syllable_split,
    part_of_speech = excluded.part_of_speech,
    category = excluded.category,
    difficulty_level = excluded.difficulty_level;
""")

# word_sounds limited core mappings
sound_map = {
    "word_water":"sound_w",
    "word_we":"sound_w",
    "word_yes":"sound_i_short",
    "word_rice":"sound_r",
    "word_light":"sound_l",
    "word_right":"sound_r",
    "word_very":"sound_v" if False else None,
}
# manual broader mapping
manual_pairs = [
    ("word_bag","sound_b"),("word_bed","sound_b") if False else None,
]
# sentences
sentences = [
    ("sentence_this_is_a_bag","This is a bag.","นี่คือกระเป๋า","pattern_this_is_blank"),

    ("sentence_i_need_help","I need help.","ฉันต้องการความช่วยเหลือ","pattern_i_need_blank"),
    ("sentence_i_like_tea","I like tea.","ฉันชอบชา","pattern_i_like_blank"),
    ("sentence_i_like_chicken","I like chicken.","ฉันชอบไก่","pattern_i_like_blank"),
    ("sentence_where_is_the_bathroom","Where is the bathroom?","ห้องน้ำอยู่ที่ไหน","pattern_where_is_blank"),
    ("sentence_where_is_my_bag","Where is my bag?","กระเป๋าของฉันอยู่ที่ไหน","pattern_where_is_blank"),
    ("sentence_do_you_want_water","Do you want water?","คุณต้องการน้ำไหม","pattern_do_you_want_blank"),
    ("sentence_can_you_help_me","Can you help me?","คุณช่วยฉันได้ไหม","pattern_can_you_help_me"),
    ("sentence_yes_please","Yes, please.","ค่ะ/ครับ ได้เลย","pattern_it_is_blank"),
    ("sentence_no_thank_you","No, thank you.","ไม่ ขอบคุณ","pattern_it_is_blank"),
    ("sentence_good_morning","Good morning.","สวัสดีตอนเช้า","pattern_it_is_blank"),
    ("sentence_open_the_door","Open the door.","เปิดประตู","pattern_it_is_blank"),
    ("sentence_close_the_window","Close the window.","ปิดหน้าต่าง","pattern_it_is_blank"),
]
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- SENTENCES")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for sk, en, th, psk in sentences:
    lines.append(f"""
insert into sentences (stable_key, english_text, thai_text, sentence_pattern_id, difficulty_level)
select '{sk}', '{en.replace("'", "''")}', '{th}', sp.id, 'beginner'
from sentence_patterns sp
where sp.stable_key = '{psk}'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set english_text = excluded.english_text,
    thai_text = excluded.thai_text,
    sentence_pattern_id = excluded.sentence_pattern_id,
    difficulty_level = excluded.difficulty_level;
""")

# Link sentence words for selected core sentences
sentence_word_links = {
    "sentence_i_want_water":["word_i","word_want","word_water"],
    "sentence_i_want_rice":["word_i","word_want","word_rice"],
    "sentence_i_want_tea":["word_i","word_want","word_tea"],
    "sentence_i_need_help":["word_i","word_need","word_help"],
    "sentence_i_like_tea":["word_i","word_like","word_tea"],
    "sentence_i_like_chicken":["word_i","word_like","word_chicken"],
    "sentence_where_is_the_bathroom":["word_where","word_bathroom"],
    "sentence_where_is_my_bag":["word_where","word_bag"],
    "sentence_do_you_want_water":["word_you","word_want","word_water"],
    "sentence_can_you_help_me":["word_you","word_help"],
}
for ssk, wlist in sentence_word_links.items():
    for idx, wsk in enumerate(wlist, start=1):
        lines.append(f"""
insert into sentence_words (sentence_id, word_id, display_order)
select s.id, w.id, {idx}
from sentences s, words w
where s.stable_key = '{ssk}' and w.stable_key = '{wsk}'
on conflict (sentence_id, word_id) do update
set display_order = excluded.display_order;
""")

# Lessons 60
lesson_titles = {
1:"Bag and Pen",2:"Book and Dog",3:"Cup and Room",4:"B P M Sounds",5:"Tea and Door",
6:"Go and Come",7:"See and Rice",8:"Fish and Food",9:"Water and Yes",10:"Rice and Milk",
11:"I You He She",12:"This and That",13:"Family Words",14:"Home and Friend",15:"Who Is He",

26:"Like and Love",27:"Chicken and Fruit",28:"Hot and Cold",29:"Do You Want",30:"Food Talk",
31:"Numbers 1 to 10",32:"Numbers and Money",33:"Cheap and Expensive",34:"How Much Is It",35:"Shopping Talk",
36:"What Who Where",37:"When Why How",38:"Question Practice 1",39:"Question Practice 2",40:"Simple Answers",
41:"R and L",42:"V and W",43:"TH Sound",44:"Final Consonants",45:"Stress Practice",
46:"Left Right Straight",47:"Places",48:"Car Bus Taxi",49:"Asking Directions",50:"Outside Talk",
51:"Phone Basics",52:"Morning and Night",53:"Today Tomorrow Yesterday",54:"Daily Routine",55:"Phone Talk",
56:"My Name Is",57:"My Family and Home",58:"Food and Needs",59:"Daily Conversation",60:"Final Speaking Test"
}
sound_focus_by_lesson = {
    1:"sound_b",2:"sound_i_short",3:"sound_u_short",4:"sound_b",5:"sound_t",
    6:"sound_g",7:"sound_s",8:"sound_f",9:"sound_w",10:"sound_rice" if False else "sound_w",
    11:"sound_i_short",12:"sound_th_voiced",13:"sound_f",14:"sound_h" if False else "sound_m",
    15:"sound_h" if False else "sound_who" if False else "sound_w",
    16:"sound_r",17:"sound_d",18:"sound_s",19:"sound_e_short",20:"sound_h" if False else "sound_o_short",
    21:"sound_happy" if False else "sound_a_short",22:"sound_th_unvoiced",23:"sound_i_short",24:"sound_n",25:"sound_i_short",
    26:"sound_l",27:"sound_ch",28:"sound_h",29:"sound_w",30:"sound_f",
    31:"sound_w",32:"sound_thirty" if False else "sound_th_unvoiced",33:"sound_ch",34:"sound_h",35:"sound_sh",
    36:"sound_w",37:"sound_how" if False else "sound_h",38:"sound_w",39:"sound_w",40:"sound_m",
    41:"sound_r",42:"sound_v",43:"sound_th_unvoiced",44:"sound_ng",45:"sound_a_short",
    46:"sound_l",47:"sound_m",48:"sound_t",49:"sound_w",50:"sound_s",
    51:"sound_k",52:"sound_m",53:"sound_t",54:"sound_w",55:"sound_h",
    56:"sound_m",57:"sound_f",58:"sound_f",59:"sound_w",60:"sound_w",
}
# Normalize to existing sound keys
valid_sound_keys = {s[0] for s in sounds}
for k,v in list(sound_focus_by_lesson.items()):
    if v not in valid_sound_keys:
        sound_focus_by_lesson[k] = "sound_w"

lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- LESSONS")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for lesson_num in range(1,61):
    week = ((lesson_num-1)//5)+1 if lesson_num <= 60 else 12
    if lesson_num in [6,13,20,27,34,41,48,55]:
        week = ((lesson_num-1)//5)+1
    unit_key = f"unit_week_{((lesson_num-1)//5)+1 if lesson_num <= 60 else 12}"
    order_in_week = ((lesson_num-1)%5)+1 if lesson_num <= 60 else 5
    title = lesson_titles[lesson_num]
    sf = sound_focus_by_lesson[lesson_num]
    lines.append(f"""
insert into lessons (stable_key, unit_id, lesson_order, title, subtitle, estimated_minutes, lesson_type, sound_focus_id, is_review_lesson, is_published)
select 'lesson_{lesson_num:03d}', u.id, {order_in_week}, '{title.replace("'", "''")}', null, 12, 'standard', s.id, false, true
from units u
left join sounds s on s.stable_key = '{sf}'
where u.stable_key = '{unit_key}'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    lesson_order = excluded.lesson_order,
    estimated_minutes = excluded.estimated_minutes,
    lesson_type = excluded.lesson_type,
    sound_focus_id = excluded.sound_focus_id,
    is_published = excluded.is_published;
""")

# Attach target words to first 12 lessons more richly, rest lightly
lesson_word_map = {
    1:["word_bag","word_pen","word_bed","word_cat"] if False else ["word_bag","word_pen","word_book","word_bed"],
    2:["word_book","word_dog"] if False else ["word_book","word_big","word_box","word_sit"],
    3:["word_cup","word_room","word_good","word_bus"],
    4:["word_baby","word_mother","word_pen","word_bag"],
    5:["word_ten","word_door","word_tea","word_day"] if False else ["word_ten","word_door","word_tea","word_no"],
    6:["word_go","word_come","word_home","word_good"],
    7:["word_see","word_rice","word_sun"] if False else ["word_see","word_rice","word_good","word_yes"],
    8:["word_fish","word_five","word_food","word_very"] if False else ["word_fish","word_five","word_food","word_friend"],
    9:["word_water","word_yes","word_you","word_we","word_yellow"],
    10:["word_rice","word_milk","word_egg","word_soup","word_bread"],
    11:["word_i","word_you","word_he","word_she","word_we"],
    12:["word_this","word_that","word_here","word_there","word_it"],
}
default_week_words = [
    "word_water","word_rice","word_help","word_happy","word_friend",
    "word_house","word_room","word_mother","word_tea","word_bag"
]
for lesson_num in range(1,61):
    words_for = lesson_word_map.get(lesson_num, default_week_words[:4])
    for idx,wsk in enumerate(words_for, start=1):
        lines.append(f"""
insert into lesson_words (lesson_id, word_id, display_order)
select l.id, w.id, {idx}
from lessons l, words w
where l.stable_key = 'lesson_{lesson_num:03d}' and w.stable_key = '{wsk}'
on conflict (lesson_id, word_id) do update
set display_order = excluded.display_order;
""")

# Attach 1-2 sentences to each lesson

for lesson_num, sents in lesson_sentence_pairs.items():
    for idx,ssk in enumerate(sents, start=1):
        lines.append(f"""
insert into lesson_sentences (lesson_id, sentence_id, display_order)
select l.id, s.id, {idx}
from lessons l, sentences s
where l.stable_key = 'lesson_{lesson_num:03d}' and s.stable_key = '{ssk}'
on conflict (lesson_id, sentence_id) do update
set display_order = excluded.display_order;
""")

# Lesson steps template for all lessons
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- LESSON STEPS")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
step_templates = [
    (1,"audio_listen","Listen","ฟัง","{\"mode\":\"sound_focus\"}","{\"auto_pass_after_play\":true}"),
    (2,"syllable_drill","Say the syllables","พูดตามพยางค์","{\"mode\":\"syllable_drill\"}","{\"min_attempts\":1}"),
    (3,"word_flashcard","Learn the words","เรียนคำศัพท์","{\"mode\":\"word_flashcards\"}","{\"min_cards\":4}"),
    (4,"speak_sentence","Say the sentence","พูดประโยค","{\"mode\":\"sentence_speak\"}","{\"min_attempts\":1}"),
    (5,"dialogue_turn","Mini dialogue","บทสนทนาสั้น","{\"mode\":\"mini_dialogue\"}","{\"min_attempts\":1}")
]
for lesson_num in range(1,61):
    for step_order, step_type, en, th, payload, passing in step_templates:
        lines.append(f"""
insert into lesson_steps (stable_key, lesson_id, step_order, step_type, instruction_en, instruction_th, payload_json, passing_rule_json)
select 'lesson_{lesson_num:03d}_step_{step_order:03d}', l.id, {step_order}, '{step_type}', '{en}', '{th}', '{payload}'::jsonb, '{passing}'::jsonb
from lessons l
where l.stable_key = 'lesson_{lesson_num:03d}'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set step_order = excluded.step_order,
    step_type = excluded.step_type,
    instruction_en = excluded.instruction_en,
    instruction_th = excluded.instruction_th,
    payload_json = excluded.payload_json,
    passing_rule_json = excluded.passing_rule_json;
""")

# Dialogues
dialogues = [
    ("dialogue_greetings_001","Greetings","Simple hello and introduction","greetings","guided"),
    ("dialogue_home_001","At Home","Simple home conversation","home","guided"),
    ("dialogue_food_001","Ordering Water","Practice asking for a drink","food","guided"),
    ("dialogue_food_002","Ordering Rice","Practice asking for food","food","guided"),
    ("dialogue_help_001","Asking for Help","Practice asking for help","help","guided"),
    ("dialogue_directions_001","Bathroom Directions","Practice asking for the bathroom","directions","guided"),
    ("dialogue_phone_001","Phone Basics","Simple phone call conversation","phone","guided"),
    ("dialogue_feelings_001","How Are You","Talk about feelings","feelings","guided"),
]
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- DIALOGUES")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for sk, title, desc, ctx, mode in dialogues:
    phrases = json.dumps(["Hello.","How are you?","I want water.","Yes, please."])
    lines.append(f"""
insert into dialogues (stable_key, title, description, context_type, mode, level_id, target_phrases, validation_json, is_published)
select '{sk}', '{title}', '{desc}', '{ctx}', '{mode}', l.id, '{phrases}'::jsonb, '{{}}'::jsonb, true
from levels l
where l.stable_key = 'level_0'
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    description = excluded.description,
    context_type = excluded.context_type,
    mode = excluded.mode,
    level_id = excluded.level_id,
    target_phrases = excluded.target_phrases,
    is_published = excluded.is_published;
""")

dialogue_turns = {
    "dialogue_greetings_001":[
        ("app","Hello.","สวัสดี",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Hello.","Hi."],"Say: Hello."),
        ("app","How are you?","สบายดีไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["I am fine.","Fine, thank you."],"Say: I am fine.")
    ],
    "dialogue_home_001":[
        ("app","Where are you?","คุณอยู่ที่ไหน",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["I am at home.","I am in the room."],"Say: I am at home."),
        ("app","Come here, please.","มานี่หน่อย",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Okay.","Yes."],"Say: Okay.")
    ],
    "dialogue_food_001":[
        ("app","Do you want water?","คุณต้องการน้ำไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Yes, please.","Yes please."],"Say: Yes, please."),
        ("app","Here you are.","นี่ค่ะ/ครับ",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Thank you.","Thanks."],"Say: Thank you.")
    ],
    "dialogue_food_002":[
        ("app","What do you want to eat?","คุณอยากกินอะไร",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["I want rice.","Rice, please."],"Say: I want rice."),
        ("app","Do you want chicken?","คุณต้องการไก่ไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Yes, please.","No, thank you."],"Say: Yes, please.")
    ],
    "dialogue_help_001":[
        ("app","Are you okay?","คุณโอเคไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["I need help.","Can you help me?"],"Say: I need help."),
        ("app","Yes, I can help.","ได้ ฉันช่วยได้",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Thank you.","Thank you very much."],"Say: Thank you.")
    ],
    "dialogue_directions_001":[
        ("app","Excuse me, where is the bathroom?","ขอโทษ ห้องน้ำอยู่ที่ไหน",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Where is the bathroom?"],"Say: Where is the bathroom?"),
        ("app","Go straight. Turn left.","ตรงไป แล้วเลี้ยวซ้าย",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Thank you.","Okay, thank you."],"Say: Thank you.")
    ],
    "dialogue_phone_001":[
        ("app","Hello?","ฮัลโหล",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Hello."],"Say: Hello."),
        ("app","Can you hear me?","ได้ยินฉันไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Yes, I can hear you.","I can hear you."],"Say: Yes, I can hear you.")
    ],
    "dialogue_feelings_001":[
        ("app","How are you?","คุณสบายดีไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["I am happy.","I am tired.","I am fine."],"Say: I am fine."),
        ("app","Are you hungry?","คุณหิวไหม",None,None),
        ("learner",None,None,["Yes, I am.","No, I am not."],"Say: Yes, I am.")
    ]
}
for dsk, turns in dialogue_turns.items():
    for order, (speaker, text, thai, expected, hint) in enumerate(turns, start=1):
        txt = "null" if text is None else "'" + text.replace("'", "''") + "'"
        th = "null" if thai is None else "'" + thai.replace("'", "''") + "'"
        exp = "null" if expected is None else "'" + json.dumps(expected).replace("'", "''") + "'::jsonb"
        hint_sql = "null" if hint is None else "'" + hint.replace("'", "''") + "'"
        validation = "null" if expected is None else "'exact_or_normalized'"
        lines.append(f"""
insert into dialogue_turns (dialogue_id, turn_order, speaker, text, thai_text, expected_answers, validation_type, hint_text)
select d.id, {order}, '{speaker}', {txt}, {th}, {exp}, {validation}, {hint_sql}
from dialogues d
where d.stable_key = '{dsk}'
on conflict (dialogue_id, turn_order) do update
set speaker = excluded.speaker,
    text = excluded.text,
    thai_text = excluded.thai_text,
    expected_answers = excluded.expected_answers,
    validation_type = excluded.validation_type,
    hint_text = excluded.hint_text;
""")

# Achievements
achievements = [
    ("first_lesson_complete","First Lesson Complete","Completed the first lesson"),
    ("seven_day_streak","7-Day Streak","Practiced 7 days in a row"),
    ("hundred_words","100 Words","Learned 100 words"),
    ("first_dialogue_complete","First Dialogue Complete","Completed the first dialogue"),
]
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- ACHIEVEMENTS")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for code,title,desc in achievements:
    lines.append(f"""
insert into achievements (code, title, description)
values ('{code}', '{title}', '{desc}')
on conflict (code) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    description = excluded.description;
""")

# Download packs
packs = [
    ("pack_week_1","Week 1 Audio Pack",42,120,True),
    ("pack_core_sounds","Core Sounds Pack",30,80,True),
]
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
lines.append("-- DOWNLOAD PACKS")
lines.append("-- =========================================================")
for sk,title,size,asset_count,pub in packs:
    lines.append(f"""
insert into download_packs (stable_key, title, size_mb, asset_count, is_published)
values ('{sk}', '{title}', {size}, {asset_count}, {'true' if pub else 'false'})
on conflict (stable_key) do update
set title = excluded.title,
    size_mb = excluded.size_mb,
    asset_count = excluded.asset_count,
    is_published = excluded.is_published;
""")

lines.append("commit;")
seed_sql = "\n".join(lines)

path = Path('/mnt/data/easy-english-thai-seed-data.sql')
path.write_text(seed_sql, encoding='utf-8')
print(f"Wrote {path} ({path.stat().st_size} bytes)")
```

STDOUT/STDERR

undefined

Done: easy-english-thai-seed-data.sql

It seeds:

*   course and level
*   12 weekly modules and units
*   60 lessons
*   core sound inventory
*   starter word library
*   sentence patterns
*   starter sentences
*   lesson-word and lesson-sentence links
*   lesson step templates
*   starter dialogues and dialogue turns
*   achievements
*   initial download packs

You now have a usable backend set:

*   OpenAPI strict spec
*   Schema
*   RLS policies
*   Storage policies
*   Seed data

## Response:
08/04/2026, 01:12:17

I’m taking the backend package and mapping it into a buildable Flutter app structure: modules, state flow, repositories, API client boundaries, and delivery order for the core screens.

> Thought for 9s

Below is a **Flutter app architecture and screen/state implementation plan** for this project.

It is designed to fit the backend artifacts already created:

*   OpenAPI spec
*   Postgres schema
*   RLS policies
*   storage policies
*   seed data

This gives you a practical build path from backend design to a real app.

* * *

1\. Technical direction
=======================

Recommended stack
-----------------

*   **Flutter**
*   **Dart**
*   **Riverpod** for state management
*   **GoRouter** for navigation
*   **Dio** for HTTP client
*   **Freezed + json\_serializable** for models
*   **Hive** or **Isar** for local cache
*   **flutter\_secure\_storage** for tokens
*   **record** for audio capture
*   **just\_audio** for playback
*   **permission\_handler** for mic permissions

Why this stack
--------------

It fits this product because you need:

*   many screen states
*   strong offline/local caching
*   clean API integration
*   fast iteration
*   stable audio recording/playback

* * *

2\. App architecture style
==========================

Use **feature-first clean architecture**.

Top-level layers
----------------

*   `app`
*   `core`
*   `features`
*   `shared`

Clean separation
----------------

Each feature should have:

*   `data`
*   `domain`
*   `presentation`

That gives:

*   less coupling
*   easier testing
*   easier replacement of API or storage later

* * *


Use this same structure for all features.

Complex interaction screens

Use explicit state classes

Examples:

*   lesson player
*   dialogue session
*   review session
*   recording/pronunciation flow

9\. Screen state models
=======================

9.1 Lesson player state
-----------------------

```
class LessonPlayerState {
  final Lesson lesson;
  final List<LessonStep> steps;
  final int currentStepIndex;
  final LessonStepUiState stepUiState;
  final bool isAudioPlaying;
  final bool isRecording;
  final bool isProcessingSpeech;
  final String? transcript;
  final PronunciationResult? pronunciationResult;
  final int completionPercent;
  final String? errorMessage;
}
```

9.2 Step UI state
-----------------

Use a sealed state:

*   idle
*   listening
*   readyToRecord
*   recording
*   processing
*   answeredCorrectly
*   answeredIncorrectly
*   completed

9.3 Dialogue session state
--------------------------

```
class DialogueSessionState {
  final Dialogue dialogue;
  final String sessionId;
  final List<DialogueTurnViewModel> turns;
  final int currentTurnIndex;
  final bool isRecording;
  final bool isProcessing;
  final String? transcript;
  final String? feedback;
  final bool accepted;
  final String? hintText;
  final bool completed;
}
```

9.4 Review session state
------------------------

```
class ReviewSessionState {
  final List<ReviewQueueItem> items;
  final int currentIndex;
  final ReviewItemUi currentUi;
  final int correctCount;
  final int incorrectCount;
  final bool loadingNext;
  final bool completed;
}
```

10\. Data layer design
======================

Repository pattern
------------------

Every feature should depend on abstract repositories.

Example:

```
abstract class LessonRepository {
  Future<Lesson> getLesson(String lessonId);
  Future<List<LessonStep>> getLessonSteps(String lessonId);
  Future<LessonProgress> startLesson(String lessonId, {required String source});
  Future<void> saveStepProgress(...);
  Future<LessonCompletionResult> completeLesson(...);
}
```

Implementation:

```
class LessonRepositoryImpl implements LessonRepository {
  final LessonRemoteDataSource remote;
  final LessonLocalDataSource local;
}
```

* * *

11\. DTO and entity mapping
===========================

DTO layer
---------

Match API response exactly.

Example:

*   `LessonDto`
*   `LessonStepDto`
*   `WordDto`

Domain entities
---------------

Cleaner app model:

*   `Lesson`
*   `LessonStep`
*   `Word`
*   `Sentence`
*   `Dialogue`

Mapper rule
-----------

Never pass DTOs directly into widgets.

12\. API client design
======================

Use `Dio`.

Required interceptors
---------------------

*   auth token interceptor
*   refresh token interceptor
*   request logging
*   retry policy for transient failures

API error mapping
-----------------

Map raw HTTP failures into typed app errors:

*   `NetworkFailure`
*   `UnauthorizedFailure`
*   `ValidationFailure`
*   `SpeechProcessingFailure`
*   `ServerFailure`

=================================

Cache locally
-------------

*   course map
*   lesson detail
*   lesson steps
*   words
*   sounds
*   dialogues metadata
*   download manifests

Do not rely on stale cache for

*   review queue
*   home recommendation
*   progress summary
*   live speech scores

Local DB tables
---------------

Suggested local cache collections:

*   cached\_lessons
*   cached\_lesson\_steps
*   cached\_words
*   cached\_sentences
*   cached\_sounds
*   cached\_dialogues
*   downloaded\_packs
*   pending\_analytics\_events

14\. Audio architecture
=======================

Audio player service
--------------------

Responsibilities:

*   play normal audio
*   play slow audio

*   expose playback state

Methods:

```
playUrl(String url)
playAsset(String path)
stop()
pause()
resume()
```

-----------------------

Responsibilities:

*   request mic permission
*   start recording
*   stop recording
*   return local file path

Methods:

```
Future<bool> ensurePermission()
Future<void> startRecording()
Future<String> stopRecording()
```

Speech session service
----------------------

Responsibilities:

*   upload recording
*   transcribe
*   request pronunciation scoring
*   return structured result

Methods:

```
Future<SpeechUploadResult> uploadRecording(String path)
Future<TranscriptResult> transcribe(String assetUrl, SpeechContext context)
Future<PronunciationResult> scoreWord(...)
Future<PronunciationResult> scoreSentence(...)
Future<PronunciationResult> scoreSound(...)
```

15\. Lesson player rendering system
===================================

This is important.

Use a **step renderer factory**.

Lesson step renderer
--------------------

```
Widget buildStep(LessonStep step) {
  switch (step.stepType) {
    case StepType.audioListen:
      return AudioListenStep(...);
    case StepType.syllableDrill:
      return SyllableDrillStep(...);
    case StepType.wordFlashcard:
      return WordFlashcardStep(...);
    case StepType.speakSentence:
      return SpeakSentenceStep(...);
    case StepType.dialogueTurn:
      return DialogueTurnStep(...);
  }
}
```

This keeps the lesson engine extensible.

17\. Navigation state rules
===========================

Bottom tabs keep stack
----------------------

Each main tab should preserve state:

*   Home
*   Review
*   Sounds
*   Speak
*   Profile

Lesson flow should be isolated
------------------------------

Once in lesson:

*   intro
*   player
*   completion

Use one controller lifecycle per lesson session.

* * *

18\. Error handling strategy
============================

Network failure
---------------

Show:

*   inline retry
*   fallback cached data if safe

Speech failure
--------------

Show:

*   “Try again”
*   “Skip this speaking step”
*   do not block entire lesson unless required

Auth failure
------------

Refresh once automatically.  
If still invalid:

*   logout
*   send to login/guest bootstrap

Permission denied
-----------------

Show:

*   why mic is needed
*   open settings action
*   continue without voice where possible

* * *

19\. Analytics instrumentation plan
===================================

Instrument at controller level.

Track these
-----------

*   app open
*   home viewed
*   lesson started
*   lesson step viewed
*   audio replay tapped
*   recording started/stopped
*   transcription success/fail
*   pronunciation score received
*   lesson completed
*   review completed
*   dialogue completed
*   setting changed
*   pack downloaded

Implementation
--------------

Use an `AnalyticsService` with batched background flush.

* * *

20\. Dependency injection plan
==============================

Use Riverpod providers.

Example
-------

```
final dioProvider = Provider<Dio>((ref) => buildDio(ref));
final authRepositoryProvider = Provider<AuthRepository>((ref) {
  return AuthRepositoryImpl(ref.read(authRemoteDataSourceProvider));
});
final lessonRepositoryProvider = Provider<LessonRepository>((ref) {
  return LessonRepositoryImpl(
    ref.read(lessonRemoteDataSourceProvider),
    ref.read(lessonLocalDataSourceProvider),
  );
});
```

* * *

21\. Recommended model generation pipeline
==========================================

Use:

*   `freezed`
*   `json_serializable`
*   `build_runner`

For:

*   DTOs
*   API response wrappers
*   immutable states where useful

This reduces API integration errors.

29\. Critical technical risks
=============================

Speech latency
--------------

Risk:

*   slow scoring disrupts learning flow

Mitigation:

*   show fast processing state
*   allow fallback retry
*   cache transcript and score results locally after completion

Audio complexity
----------------

Risk:

*   playback and recording conflicts

Mitigation:

*   centralize audio ownership in one service
*   force stop playback before recording starts

State explosion in lesson flow
------------------------------

Risk:

*   lesson player becomes unmaintainable

Mitigation:

*   use sealed state or explicit step subcontrollers
*   keep step renderer separated from controller

Offline inconsistency
---------------------

Risk:

*   stale lesson/review data

Mitigation:

*   cache content only
*   keep progress/review server-authoritative

* * *

```
lib/features/lessons/presentation/screens/lesson_player_screen.dart

```

*   dialogues
