## Prompt:
08/04/2026, 01:17:03

Firebase/Firestore schema version

## Response:
08/04/2026, 01:17:04

> Thought for 4s

Below is the **Firebase / Firestore schema version** of the backend design.

This is the NoSQL mapping of the Postgres/Supabase schema into:

*   **Firebase Authentication**
*   **Cloud Firestore**
*   **Firebase Storage**
*   optional **Cloud Functions**

This is not a 1:1 SQL copy. Firestore works best when data is shaped around:

*   read patterns
*   screen payloads
*   denormalized documents
*   small subcollections
*   explicit duplication where useful

For this app, Firestore is workable for MVP, but you should accept some denormalization.

* * *

1\. Firebase architecture
=========================

Use these Firebase products
---------------------------

*   **Firebase Auth**
*   **Cloud Firestore**
*   **Firebase Storage**
*   **Cloud Functions**
*   **Firebase Cloud Messaging**
*   **Firebase Analytics**

Auth strategy
-------------

Use Firebase Auth for:

*   anonymous guest login
*   email/password login
*   later: Google/Apple optional

Map:

*   Firebase Auth UID = primary user identity
*   use that UID as document ID in `users/{uid}`

* * *

2\. Firestore design principles for this app
============================================

Rules
-----

*   keep learner-owned data under `users/{uid}`
*   keep published learning content under top-level collections
*   duplicate summary fields needed for fast screens
*   do not force relational joins in client
*   precompute some home/review/progress summaries

Important Firestore tradeoff
----------------------------

Firestore is not ideal for:

*   heavy relational joins
*   complex server-side filtering across many linked tables

So for this app:

*   content is mostly read-only and denormalized
*   learner progress is user-scoped
*   review queues are precomputed
*   Cloud Functions can maintain derived summaries

* * *

3\. Top-level collection map
============================

Recommended top-level collections:

```
users/{uid}
courses/{courseId}
levels/{levelId}
modules/{moduleId}
units/{unitId}
lessons/{lessonId}
sounds/{soundId}
words/{wordId}
sentences/{sentenceId}
sentencePatterns/{patternId}
dialogues/{dialogueId}
minimalPairGroups/{groupId}
downloadPacks/{packId}
achievements/{achievementId}
appConfig/{docId}
analyticsEvents/{eventId}   // optional, often better sent to Analytics/BigQuery
contentQaIssues/{issueId}   // admin only
```

For learner-specific data, prefer subcollections under user:

```
users/{uid}/settings/{doc}
users/{uid}/onboardingSessions/{sessionId}
users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}
users/{uid}/wordProgress/{wordId}
users/{uid}/soundProgress/{soundId}
users/{uid}/sentenceProgress/{sentenceId}
users/{uid}/dialogueSessions/{sessionId}
users/{uid}/speakingAttempts/{attemptId}
users/{uid}/reviewQueue/{reviewId}
users/{uid}/achievements/{achievementId}
users/{uid}/deviceTokens/{tokenId}
users/{uid}/downloads/{packId}
users/{uid}/reminders/{doc}
```

* * *

4\. Core content schema
=======================

These collections are mostly global and published content.

* * *

4.1 `courses/{courseId}`
========================

Example doc:

```
{
  "id": "course_en_for_thai_beginner",
  "title": "Beginner English for Thai Speakers",
  "description": "Pronunciation-first beginner English course for Thai-speaking learners",
  "sourceLanguage": "th",
  "targetLanguage": "en",
  "version": 1,
  "isPublished": true,
  "levelIds": ["level_0"],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

Use `courseId` like:

```
course_en_for_thai_beginner
```

* * *

4.2 `levels/{levelId}`
======================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "level_0",
  "courseId": "course_en_for_thai_beginner",
  "order": 1,
  "title": "Absolute Beginner",
  "description": "Starts from zero with sounds, syllables, small words, and short sentences",
  "moduleIds": [
    "module_week_1",
    "module_week_2"
  ],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.3 `modules/{moduleId}`
========================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "module_week_1",
  "levelId": "level_0",
  "order": 1,
  "title": "Week 1",
  "description": "Week 1 learning module",
  "unitIds": ["unit_week_1"],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.4 `units/{unitId}`
====================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "unit_week_1",
  "moduleId": "module_week_1",
  "order": 1,
  "title": "Week 1 Unit",
  "description": "Primary unit for week 1",
  "lessonIds": [
    "lesson_001",
    "lesson_002",
    "lesson_003",
    "lesson_004",
    "lesson_005"
  ],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.5 `lessons/{lessonId}`
========================

This should include summary content needed for intro and listing screens.

Example:

```
{
  "id": "lesson_009",
  "unitId": "unit_week_2",
  "courseId": "course_en_for_thai_beginner",
  "levelId": "level_0",
  "weekNumber": 2,
  "lessonOrder": 4,
  "title": "Water and Yes",
  "subtitle": "Practice W sound",
  "estimatedMinutes": 12,
  "lessonType": "standard",
  "soundFocus": {
    "id": "sound_w",
    "label": "W"
  },
  "isReviewLesson": false,
  "isPublished": true,
  "targetWordIds": [
    "word_water",
    "word_yes",
    "word_you",
    "word_we",
    "word_yellow"
  ],
  "targetSentenceIds": [
    "sentence_i_want_water",
    "sentence_yes_please"
  ],
  "stepCount": 5,
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

### Subcollection for steps

Use:

```
lessons/{lessonId}/steps/{stepId}
```

Example:

```
{
  "id": "lesson_009_step_001",
  "stepOrder": 1,
  "stepType": "audio_listen",
  "title": null,
  "instructionEn": "Listen",
  "instructionTh": "ฟังเสียง",
  "payload": {
    "mode": "sound_focus",
    "soundId": "sound_w",
    "audioUrl": "gs://.../sounds/sound_w/normal.mp3"
  },
  "passingRule": {
    "autoPassAfterPlay": true
  }
}
```

* * *

4.6 `sounds/{soundId}`
======================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "sound_w",
  "soundCode": "w",
  "displaySymbol": "W",
  "title": "W sound",
  "descriptionTh": "เสียง ว",
  "mouthHint": "เริ่มด้วยริมฝีปากกลมเล็กน้อย",
  "category": "consonant",
  "thaiDifficultyFlag": true,
  "audioDemoNormalUrl": "gs://lesson-audio/sounds/sound_w/normal.mp3",
  "audioDemoSlowUrl": "gs://lesson-audio/sounds/sound_w/slow.mp3",
  "exampleWords": [
    {
      "id": "word_water",
      "englishText": "water",
      "thaiText": "น้ำ"
    }
  ],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.7 `words/{wordId}`
====================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "word_water",
  "englishText": "water",
  "thaiText": "น้ำ",
  "transliteration": null,
  "pronunciationHint": "WAW-ter",
  "ipa": "ˈwɔː.tər",
  "syllableSplit": ["wa", "ter"],
  "partOfSpeech": "noun",
  "category": "drink",
  "difficultyLevel": "beginner",
  "frequencyRank": 10,
  "imageUrl": "gs://lesson-images/words/word_water/main.png",
  "audioNormalUrl": "gs://lesson-audio/words/word_water/normal.mp3",
  "audioSlowUrl": "gs://lesson-audio/words/word_water/slow.mp3",
  "soundIds": ["sound_w"],
  "exampleSentence": {
    "id": "sentence_i_want_water",
    "englishText": "I want water.",
    "thaiText": "ฉันต้องการน้ำ"
  },
  "lessonIds": ["lesson_009"],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.8 `sentences/{sentenceId}`
============================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "sentence_i_want_water",
  "englishText": "I want water.",
  "thaiText": "ฉันต้องการน้ำ",
  "pronunciationHint": "ai want WAW-ter",
  "ipa": null,
  "sentencePatternId": "pattern_i_want_blank",
  "difficultyLevel": "beginner",
  "audioNormalUrl": "gs://lesson-audio/sentences/sentence_i_want_water/normal.mp3",
  "audioSlowUrl": "gs://lesson-audio/sentences/sentence_i_want_water/slow.mp3",
  "targetWordIds": ["word_i", "word_want", "word_water"],
  "lessonIds": ["lesson_009"],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.9 `sentencePatterns/{patternId}`
==================================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "pattern_i_want_blank",
  "patternText": "I want ___.",
  "patternTextTh": "ฉันต้องการ___",
  "explanationTh": "ใช้บอกสิ่งที่ต้องการ",
  "difficultyLevel": "beginner",
  "exampleSentenceIds": [
    "sentence_i_want_water",
    "sentence_i_want_rice",
    "sentence_i_want_tea"
  ],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.10 `dialogues/{dialogueId}`
=============================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "dialogue_food_001",
  "title": "Ordering Water",
  "description": "Practice asking for a drink",
  "contextType": "food",
  "mode": "guided",
  "levelId": "level_0",
  "isPublished": true,
  "targetPhrases": [
    "I want water.",
    "Yes, please."
  ],
  "validationConfig": {},
  "turnCount": 4,
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

### Subcollection

```
dialogues/{dialogueId}/turns/{turnId}
```

Example:

```
{
  "id": "turn_002",
  "turnOrder": 2,
  "speaker": "learner",
  "text": null,
  "thaiText": null,
  "audioUrl": null,
  "expectedAnswers": [
    "Yes, please.",
    "Yes please."
  ],
  "validationType": "exact_or_normalized",
  "hintText": "Say: Yes, please."
}
```

* * *

4.11 `minimalPairGroups/{groupId}`
==================================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "mp_r_l",
  "title": "R and L",
  "soundA": {
    "id": "sound_r",
    "displaySymbol": "R"
  },
  "soundB": {
    "id": "sound_l",
    "displaySymbol": "L"
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "id": "pair_001",
      "wordA": {
        "id": "word_right",
        "englishText": "right",
        "thaiText": "ขวา"
      },
      "wordB": {
        "id": "word_light",
        "englishText": "light",
        "thaiText": "ไฟ"
      }
    }
  ],
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

Firestore prefers keeping the pair items embedded unless there are many.

* * *

4.12 `downloadPacks/{packId}`
=============================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "pack_week_1",
  "title": "Week 1 Audio Pack",
  "sizeMb": 42,
  "assetCount": 120,
  "isPublished": true,
  "files": [
    {
      "assetId": "asset_001",
      "url": "gs://downloadable-packs/packs/week_1/week_1_audio.zip",
      "checksum": "sha256-abc"
    }
  ],
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

4.13 `achievements/{achievementId}`
===================================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "first_lesson_complete",
  "code": "first_lesson_complete",
  "title": "First Lesson Complete",
  "description": "Completed the first lesson",
  "iconUrl": null,
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

5\. User root document schema
=============================

`users/{uid}`
-------------

This is the learner profile summary.

Example:

```
{
  "uid": "firebase_uid_123",
  "displayName": "Mali",
  "email": "user@example.com",
  "phone": null,
  "nativeLanguage": "th",
  "interfaceLanguage": "th",
  "learningGoal": "daily_life",
  "currentLevelId": "level_0",
  "currentLessonId": "lesson_009",
  "isGuest": false,
  "role": "learner",
  "homeSummary": {
    "lessonsCompleted": 8,
    "wordsLearned": 41,
    "streakDays": 6
  },
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

`homeSummary` is denormalized for fast home screen reads.

* * *

6\. User subcollections
=======================

* * *

6.1 `users/{uid}/settings/default`
==================================

Single settings doc.

Example:

```
{
  "interfaceLanguage": "th",
  "thaiTranslationEnabled": true,
  "bilingualMode": true,
  "preferredVoiceGender": "female",
  "audioSpeedDefault": "normal",
  "subtitlesEnabled": true,
  "notificationsEnabled": true,
  "dailyReminderTime": "19:00:00",
  "saveRecordings": true,
  "strictAnswerMode": false,
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

Use fixed doc ID:

```
users/{uid}/settings/default
```

* * *

6.2 `users/{uid}/onboardingSessions/{sessionId}`
================================================

Example:

```
{
  "id": "onb_001",
  "interfaceLanguage": "th",
  "learningGoal": "start_from_zero",
  "recommendedFlow": [
    "welcome",
    "account_setup",
    "level_check"
  ],
  "status": "completed",
  "recommendedLevelId": "level_0",
  "recommendedLessonId": "lesson_001",
  "createdAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

### Nested answers

Use subcollection:

```
users/{uid}/onboardingSessions/{sessionId}/answers/{questionId}
```

Example:

```
{
  "questionId": "placement_q1",
  "answer": {
    "type": "choice",
    "value": "do_not_understand"
  },
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.3 `users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}`
===========================================

Use lesson ID as doc ID.

Example:

```
{
  "lessonId": "lesson_009",
  "status": "in_progress",
  "startedAt": "timestamp",
  "completedAt": null,
  "completionPercent": 33,
  "currentStepId": "lesson_009_step_003",
  "retryCount": 2,
  "timeSpentSeconds": 184,
  "scoreOverall": null,
  "pronunciationScore": null,
  "comprehensionScore": null,
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

### Nested step progress

Use:

```
users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}/steps/{stepId}
```

Example:

```
{
  "stepId": "lesson_009_step_003",
  "status": "completed",
  "attempts": 1,
  "timeSpentSeconds": 28,
  "score": {
    "overall": 78,
    "pronunciation": 75
  },
  "responseSummary": {
    "selectedAnswer": "น้ำ",
    "recognizedText": null
  },
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.4 `users/{uid}/wordProgress/{wordId}`
=======================================

Example:

```
{
  "wordId": "word_water",
  "familiarityScore": 72,
  "pronunciationScore": 69,
  "listeningScore": 80,
  "speakingScore": 68,
  "timesSeen": 6,
  "timesCorrect": 5,
  "timesIncorrect": 1,
  "lastSeenAt": "timestamp",
  "nextReviewAt": "timestamp",
  "isHardWord": false,
  "isFavorite": true,
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.5 `users/{uid}/soundProgress/{soundId}`
=========================================

Example:

```
{
  "soundId": "sound_r",
  "accuracyScore": 41,
  "attemptsCount": 12,
  "lastPracticedAt": "timestamp",
  "nextReviewAt": "timestamp",
  "difficultyFlag": true,
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.6 `users/{uid}/sentenceProgress/{sentenceId}`
===============================================

Example:

```
{
  "sentenceId": "sentence_i_want_water",
  "familiarityScore": 64,
  "speakingScore": 60,
  "timesPracticed": 4,
  "nextReviewAt": "timestamp",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.7 `users/{uid}/dialogueSessions/{sessionId}`
==============================================

Example:

```
{
  "sessionId": "ds_001",
  "dialogueId": "dialogue_food_001",
  "mode": "guided",
  "status": "in_progress",
  "currentTurnId": "turn_002",
  "scoreOverall": null,
  "startedAt": "timestamp",
  "completedAt": null,
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

### Nested responses

```
users/{uid}/dialogueSessions/{sessionId}/turns/{turnId}
```

Example:

```
{
  "turnId": "turn_002",
  "transcriptText": "Yes, please.",
  "audioPath": "gs://user-recordings/users/firebase_uid_123/2026/04/uuid.m4a",
  "accepted": true,
  "score": 88,
  "feedback": "Good job.",
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.8 `users/{uid}/speakingAttempts/{attemptId}`
==============================================

Example:

```
{
  "attemptId": "attempt_001",
  "lessonStepId": "lesson_009_step_004",
  "wordId": "word_water",
  "sentenceId": null,
  "dialogueId": null,
  "recordingPath": "gs://user-recordings/users/firebase_uid_123/2026/04/uuid.m4a",
  "transcriptText": "water",
  "recognitionConfidence": 0.93,
  "pronunciationScore": 71,
  "phonemeFeedback": [
    {
      "part": "wa",
      "score": 76
    },
    {
      "part": "ter",
      "score": 63
    }
  ],
  "feedbackText": "Stress the first part: WA-ter.",
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.9 `users/{uid}/reviewQueue/{reviewId}`
========================================

Use generated doc IDs or a deterministic ID like `word_word_water`.

Example:

```
{
  "reviewId": "rq_001",
  "contentType": "word",
  "contentId": "word_water",
  "dueAt": "timestamp",
  "priority": 10,
  "sourceReason": "due_review",
  "exerciseType": "audio_to_meaning",
  "completedAt": null,
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

This collection powers the review screen directly.

* * *

6.10 `users/{uid}/achievements/{achievementId}`
===============================================

Example:

```
{
  "achievementId": "first_lesson_complete",
  "code": "first_lesson_complete",
  "title": "First Lesson Complete",
  "unlockedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

This duplicates some metadata for easier UI rendering.

* * *

6.11 `users/{uid}/deviceTokens/{tokenId}`
=========================================

Example:

```
{
  "platform": "ios",
  "deviceToken": "apns_token_here",
  "deviceId": "device_abc123",
  "createdAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

6.12 `users/{uid}/downloads/{packId}`
=====================================

Example:

```
{
  "packId": "pack_week_1",
  "isDownloaded": true,
  "downloadedAt": "timestamp",
  "version": 1
}
```

Mostly optional if client stores download metadata locally.

* * *

6.13 `users/{uid}/reminders/default`
====================================

Example:

```
{
  "enabled": true,
  "dailyTime": "19:30:00",
  "timezone": "Asia/Bangkok",
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

7\. Home screen optimized document
==================================

For speed, use a derived document:

```
users/{uid}/derived/home
```

Example:

```
{
  "greetingName": "Mali",
  "todayLesson": {
    "id": "lesson_009",
    "title": "Water and Yes",
    "estimatedMinutes": 12,
    "progressPercent": 0,
    "cta": "start"
  },
  "reviewDue": {
    "wordCount": 8,
    "soundCount": 2,
    "sentenceCount": 3,
    "dialogueCount": 1
  },
  "recommendedPractice": {
    "type": "sound",
    "targetId": "sound_w",
    "title": "Practice W sound"
  },
  "recentWords": [
    {
      "id": "word_water",
      "englishText": "water",
      "thaiText": "น้ำ"
    }
  ],
  "summary": {
    "lessonsCompleted": 8,
    "wordsLearned": 41,
    "streakDays": 6
  },
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

This can be maintained by Cloud Functions.

* * *

8\. Progress dashboard optimized document
=========================================

Use:

```
users/{uid}/derived/progress
```

Example:

```
{
  "courseCompletionPercent": 14,
  "lessonsCompleted": 8,
  "wordsLearned": 41,
  "dialoguesCompleted": 3,
  "streakDays": 6,
  "pronunciationTrend": [
    { "week": 1, "score": 62 },
    { "week": 2, "score": 67 }
  ],
  "weakSounds": [
    {
      "soundId": "sound_r",
      "label": "R",
      "accuracyScore": 41
    }
  ],
  "updatedAt": "timestamp"
}
```

* * *

9\. Firestore query strategy
============================

Good query patterns
-------------------

*   get one lesson by ID
*   get steps subcollection ordered by `stepOrder`
*   get learner progress by ID under their own subtree
*   query review queue ordered by `dueAt`
*   query words by category
*   query dialogues by `contextType` and `isPublished`

Avoid
-----

*   relational cross-collection joins on client
*   huge array-based joins
*   trying to compute home screen from raw collections each time

* * *

10\. Recommended composite indexes
==================================

You will likely need indexes for:

Global content
--------------

*   `lessons`: `unitId + lessonOrder`
*   `lessons`: `isPublished + weekNumber`
*   `words`: `category + difficultyLevel`
*   `dialogues`: `contextType + isPublished`
*   `dialogues`: `levelId + isPublished`

User data
---------

*   `users/{uid}/reviewQueue`: `dueAt + priority`
*   `users/{uid}/wordProgress`: `nextReviewAt + isHardWord`
*   `users/{uid}/soundProgress`: `nextReviewAt + difficultyFlag`
*   `users/{uid}/lessonProgress`: `status + updatedAt`

* * *

11\. Firestore security rules model
===================================

Public content
--------------

Allow read to:

*   published content only

Learner data
------------

Allow read/write only to:

*   owner UID path

Admin content
-------------

Only admin users can:

*   create/update published content
*   manage QA docs
*   manage pack manifests

Storage
-------

*   public lesson media readable
*   user recordings private to owner/admin

* * *

12\. Recommended Firestore document ID strategy
===============================================

Use stable readable IDs for content:

*   `lesson_001`
*   `word_water`
*   `sentence_i_want_water`
*   `sound_w`
*   `dialogue_food_001`

Use generated IDs for:

*   attempts
*   review queue items
*   device token docs
*   onboarding sessions
*   dialogue sessions

Reason:

*   content is easier to seed and reference
*   user interaction data can scale independently

* * *

13\. Derived data strategy with Cloud Functions
===============================================

Use Cloud Functions for:

*   update `users/{uid}/derived/home`
*   update `users/{uid}/derived/progress`
*   create review queue items after progress changes
*   unlock achievements
*   maintain streaks
*   optionally validate publishable content

Trigger examples
----------------

*   on `lessonProgress/{lessonId}` write
*   on `wordProgress/{wordId}` write
*   on `soundProgress/{soundId}` write
*   on `dialogueSessions/{sessionId}` completion
*   scheduled function for daily review reminders

* * *

14\. Firebase Storage layout
============================

Buckets / folders
-----------------

If using default Firebase Storage bucket, use folder prefixes:

```
lesson-audio/
lesson-images/
downloadable-packs/
user-recordings/
```

### Example paths

```
lesson-audio/sounds/sound_w/normal.mp3
lesson-audio/lessons/lesson_009/step_001.mp3
lesson-images/words/word_water/main.png
downloadable-packs/packs/week_1/week_1_audio.zip
user-recordings/users/{uid}/2026/04/{attemptId}.m4a
```

* * *

15\. Firestore schema summary by collection
===========================================

Global content
--------------

```
courses
levels
modules
units
lessons
lessons/{lessonId}/steps
sounds
words
sentences
sentencePatterns
dialogues
dialogues/{dialogueId}/turns
minimalPairGroups
downloadPacks
achievements
appConfig
```

Per-user
--------

```
users
users/{uid}/settings
users/{uid}/onboardingSessions
users/{uid}/lessonProgress
users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}/steps
users/{uid}/wordProgress
users/{uid}/soundProgress
users/{uid}/sentenceProgress
users/{uid}/dialogueSessions
users/{uid}/dialogueSessions/{sessionId}/turns
users/{uid}/speakingAttempts
users/{uid}/reviewQueue
users/{uid}/achievements
users/{uid}/deviceTokens
users/{uid}/downloads
users/{uid}/reminders
users/{uid}/derived
```

* * *

16\. Recommended Firebase version of home reads
===============================================

For app performance, the home screen should read:

1.  `users/{uid}`
2.  `users/{uid}/derived/home`
3.  maybe `users/{uid}/settings/default`

Not:

*   dozens of raw collections at launch

* * *

17\. Recommended Firebase version of lesson flow
================================================

To start a lesson, the app reads:

1.  `lessons/{lessonId}`
2.  `lessons/{lessonId}/steps`
3.  `users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}`
4.  maybe `users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}/steps/*`

This works well in Firestore.

* * *

18\. Recommended Firebase version of review flow
================================================

The app reads:

*   `users/{uid}/reviewQueue`  
    ordered by:
*   `dueAt asc`
*   maybe filtered by `completedAt == null`

This is much better than dynamically computing review items in client.

* * *

19\. Firestore pros and cons for this project
=============================================

Pros
----

*   fast MVP setup
*   easy auth integration
*   easy mobile sync
*   easy user-scoped data model
*   easy Cloud Functions triggers

Cons
----

*   more denormalization
*   harder admin reporting than SQL
*   harder complex curriculum queries
*   review/home derivation better handled with functions

For this app:

*   Firestore is fine for MVP
*   SQL/Supabase is cleaner for long-term content/reporting complexity

* * *

20\. Recommended next artifact
==============================

The strongest next deliverable is either:

*   a **Firestore security rules file**
*   a **Firebase seed/import JSON structure**
*   a **Cloud Functions design for derived home/progress/review queue**
*   a **Flutter Firebase repository mapping**

The best next step is the **Firestore security rules file**, because Firestore without strict rules is not production-safe.

I’m generating the Firestore rules layer now: published-content reads, owner-only learner data, and admin-only CMS access, plus Storage rules for media and private recordings.

```
rules_version = '2';

service cloud.firestore {
  match /databases/{database}/documents {

    function signedIn() {
      return request.auth != null;
    }

    function isOwner(uid) {
      return signedIn() && request.auth.uid == uid;
    }

    function isAdmin() {
      return signedIn() &&
        exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/users/$(request.auth.uid)) &&
        get(/databases/$(database)/documents/users/$(request.auth.uid)).data.role == "admin";
    }

    function isPublishedLesson(lessonId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/lessons/$(lessonId)) &&
        get(/databases/$(database)/documents/lessons/$(lessonId)).data.isPublished == true;
    }

    function isPublishedDialogue(dialogueId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/dialogues/$(dialogueId)) &&
        get(/databases/$(database)/documents/dialogues/$(dialogueId)).data.isPublished == true;
    }

    function isPublishedCourse(courseId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/courses/$(courseId)) &&
        get(/databases/$(database)/documents/courses/$(courseId)).data.isPublished == true;
    }

    function validInterfaceLanguage(v) {
      return v in ["th", "en", "bilingual"];
    }

    function validLearningGoal(v) {
      return v in ["daily_life", "home_conversation", "travel", "start_from_zero"];
    }

    function validVoiceSpeed(v) {
      return v in ["slow", "normal"];
    }

    function validDialogueMode(v) {
      return v in ["guided", "repeat", "open"];
    }

    function validLessonProgressStatus(v) {
      return v in ["not_started", "in_progress", "completed"];
    }

    function validReviewContentType(v) {
      return v in ["word", "sound", "sentence", "dialogue"];
    }

    function validReviewResult(v) {
      return v in ["correct", "incorrect", "partial", "skipped"];
    }

    match /users/{uid} {
      allow read: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();

      allow create: if isOwner(uid)
        && request.resource.data.uid == request.auth.uid
        && request.resource.data.role == "learner";

      allow update: if isOwner(uid)
        && request.resource.data.uid == resource.data.uid
        && request.resource.data.role == resource.data.role;

      allow delete: if false;

      match /settings/{docId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /onboardingSessions/{sessionId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();

        match /answers/{questionId} {
          allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
        }
      }

      match /lessonProgress/{lessonId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();

        match /steps/{stepId} {
          allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
        }
      }

      match /wordProgress/{wordId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /soundProgress/{soundId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /sentenceProgress/{sentenceId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /dialogueSessions/{sessionId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();

        match /turns/{turnId} {
          allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
        }
      }

      match /speakingAttempts/{attemptId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /reviewQueue/{reviewId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /achievements/{achievementId} {
        allow read: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
        allow write: if isAdmin();
      }

      match /deviceTokens/{tokenId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /downloads/{packId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /reminders/{docId} {
        allow read, write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      }

      match /derived/{docId} {
        allow read: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
        allow write: if isAdmin();
      }
    }

    match /courses/{courseId} {
      allow read: if resource.data.isPublished == true || isAdmin();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /levels/{levelId} {
      allow read: if isAdmin()
        || isPublishedCourse(resource.data.courseId);
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /modules/{moduleId} {
      allow read: if isAdmin()
        || (
          exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/levels/$(resource.data.levelId)) &&
          isPublishedCourse(
            get(/databases/$(database)/documents/levels/$(resource.data.levelId)).data.courseId
          )
        );
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /units/{unitId} {
      allow read: if isAdmin()
        || (
          exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/modules/$(resource.data.moduleId)) &&
          exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/levels/$(
            get(/databases/$(database)/documents/modules/$(resource.data.moduleId)).data.levelId
          )) &&
          isPublishedCourse(
            get(/databases/$(database)/documents/levels/$(
              get(/databases/$(database)/documents/modules/$(resource.data.moduleId)).data.levelId
            )).data.courseId
          )
        );
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /lessons/{lessonId} {
      allow read: if resource.data.isPublished == true || isAdmin();
      allow write: if isAdmin();

      match /steps/{stepId} {
        allow read: if isPublishedLesson(lessonId) || isAdmin();
        allow write: if isAdmin();
      }
    }

    match /sounds/{soundId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /words/{wordId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /sentences/{sentenceId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /sentencePatterns/{patternId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /dialogues/{dialogueId} {
      allow read: if resource.data.isPublished == true || isAdmin();
      allow write: if isAdmin();

      match /turns/{turnId} {
        allow read: if isPublishedDialogue(dialogueId) || isAdmin();
        allow write: if isAdmin();
      }
    }

    match /minimalPairGroups/{groupId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /downloadPacks/{packId} {
      allow read: if resource.data.isPublished == true || isAdmin();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /achievements/{achievementId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /appConfig/{docId} {
      allow read: if signedIn();
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /analyticsEvents/{eventId} {
      allow create: if signedIn();
      allow read: if isAdmin();
      allow update, delete: if false;
    }

    match /contentQaIssues/{issueId} {
      allow read, write: if isAdmin();
    }
  }
}
```

And the matching **Firebase Storage rules**:

```
rules_version = '2';

service firebase.storage {
  match /b/{bucket}/o {

    function signedIn() {
      return request.auth != null;
    }

    function isAdmin() {
      return signedIn();
    }

    function isOwner(uid) {
      return signedIn() && request.auth.uid == uid;
    }

    match /lesson-audio/{allPaths=**} {
      allow read: if true;
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /lesson-images/{allPaths=**} {
      allow read: if true;
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /downloadable-packs/{allPaths=**} {
      allow read: if true;
      allow write: if isAdmin();
    }

    match /user-recordings/users/{uid}/{year}/{month}/{fileName} {
      allow read: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      allow write: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
      allow delete: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin();
    }
  }
}
```

Recommended small adjustment
----------------------------

In production, do **not** leave `isAdmin()` in Storage as just `signedIn()`. Replace it with one of:

*   custom auth claims, or
*   a callable Cloud Function / server upload flow, or
*   strict admin-only upload through backend

Because Firebase Storage rules cannot safely do the same Firestore admin lookup pattern as neatly as Firestore rules without extra care.

Recommended collection validation rules
---------------------------------------

For stronger production safety, add field validation per collection, especially for:

*   `users/{uid}`
*   `users/{uid}/settings/default`
*   `users/{uid}/lessonProgress/{lessonId}`
*   `users/{uid}/reviewQueue/{reviewId}`
*   `lessons/{lessonId}`
*   `words/{wordId}`
*   `dialogues/{dialogueId}`

The best next artifact is a **strict Firestore rules file with field-level validation helpers**, so invalid client writes are blocked, not just unauthorized ones.

from pathlib import Path

rules = r"""rules_version = '2';

service cloud.firestore {
  match /databases/{database}/documents {

    // =====================================================
    // AUTH / ROLE HELPERS
    // =====================================================

    function signedIn() {
      return request.auth != null;
    }

    function isOwner(uid) {
      return signedIn() && request.auth.uid == uid;
    }

    function userDocPath(uid) {
      return /databases/$(database)/documents/users/$(uid);
    }

    function userExists(uid) {
      return exists(userDocPath(uid));
    }

    function userDoc(uid) {
      return get(userDocPath(uid));
    }

    function isAdmin() {
      return signedIn()
        && userExists(request.auth.uid)
        && userDoc(request.auth.uid).data.role == "admin";
    }

    // =====================================================
    // ENUM / TYPE HELPERS
    // =====================================================

    function validInterfaceLanguage(v) {
      return v in ['th', 'en', 'bilingual'];
    }

    function validLearningGoal(v) {
      return v in ['daily_life', 'home_conversation', 'travel', 'start_from_zero'];
    }

    function validVoiceSpeed(v) {
      return v in ['slow', 'normal'];
    }

    function validDialogueMode(v) {
      return v in ['guided', 'repeat', 'open'];
    }

    function validLessonType(v) {
      return v in ['standard', 'review', 'sound_focus', 'dialogue_focus'];
    }

    function validStepType(v) {
      return v in [
        'audio_listen',
        'audio_repeat',
        'syllable_drill',
        'word_flashcard',
        'image_match',
        'listen_choose',
        'speak_word',
        'speak_sentence',
        'speak_answer',
        'dialogue_turn',
        'review_quiz'
      ];
    }

    function validLessonProgressStatus(v) {
      return v in ['not_started', 'in_progress', 'completed'];
    }

    function validReviewContentType(v) {
      return v in ['word', 'sound', 'sentence', 'dialogue'];
    }

    function validReviewResult(v) {
      return v in ['correct', 'incorrect', 'partial', 'skipped'];
    }

    function validVoiceGender(v) {
      return v in ['male', 'female'];
    }

    function validDifficultyLevel(v) {
      return v in ['beginner', 'intermediate', 'advanced'];
    }

    function validSpeaker(v) {
      return v in ['app', 'learner'];
    }

    function isTimestampField(v) {
      return v is timestamp;
    }

    function isStringList(v) {
      return v is list;
    }

    // =====================================================
    // IMMUTABLE / DIFF HELPERS
    // =====================================================

    function onlyChanges(allowed) {
      return request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).changedKeys().hasOnly(allowed);
    }

    function createsWithOnly(allowed) {
      return request.resource.data.keys().hasOnly(allowed);
    }

    function requiredCreateFields(requiredKeys) {
      return request.resource.data.keys().hasAll(requiredKeys);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // PUBLISHED CONTENT HELPERS
    // =====================================================

    function coursePublished(courseId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/courses/$(courseId))
        && get(/databases/$(database)/documents/courses/$(courseId)).data.isPublished == true;
    }

    function lessonPublished(lessonId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/lessons/$(lessonId))
        && get(/databases/$(database)/documents/lessons/$(lessonId)).data.isPublished == true;
    }

    function dialoguePublished(dialogueId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/dialogues/$(dialogueId))
        && get(/databases/$(database)/documents/dialogues/$(dialogueId)).data.isPublished == true;
    }

    // =====================================================
    // USER DOCUMENT VALIDATORS
    // =====================================================

    function validUserCreate(uid) {
      return request.resource.data.uid == uid
        && request.resource.data.displayName is string
        && request.resource.data.displayName.size() > 0
        && request.resource.data.nativeLanguage is string
        && validInterfaceLanguage(request.resource.data.interfaceLanguage)
        && validLearningGoal(request.resource.data.learningGoal)
        && request.resource.data.isGuest is bool
        && request.resource.data.role == 'learner'
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary is map
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary.lessonsCompleted is int
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary.wordsLearned is int
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary.streakDays is int
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt)
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validUserUpdate(uid) {
      return request.resource.data.uid == resource.data.uid
        && request.resource.data.role == resource.data.role
        && request.resource.data.createdAt == resource.data.createdAt
        && request.resource.data.displayName is string
        && request.resource.data.displayName.size() > 0
        && request.resource.data.nativeLanguage is string
        && validInterfaceLanguage(request.resource.data.interfaceLanguage)
        && validLearningGoal(request.resource.data.learningGoal)
        && request.resource.data.isGuest is bool
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary is map
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary.lessonsCompleted is int
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary.wordsLearned is int
        && request.resource.data.homeSummary.streakDays is int
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validSettings() {
      return validInterfaceLanguage(request.resource.data.interfaceLanguage)
        && request.resource.data.thaiTranslationEnabled is bool
        && request.resource.data.bilingualMode is bool
        && validVoiceGender(request.resource.data.preferredVoiceGender)
        && validVoiceSpeed(request.resource.data.audioSpeedDefault)
        && request.resource.data.subtitlesEnabled is bool
        && request.resource.data.notificationsEnabled is bool
        && request.resource.data.dailyReminderTime is string
        && request.resource.data.saveRecordings is bool
        && request.resource.data.strictAnswerMode is bool
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validLessonProgress(lessonId) {
      return request.resource.data.lessonId == lessonId
        && validLessonProgressStatus(request.resource.data.status)
        && request.resource.data.completionPercent is int
        && request.resource.data.retryCount is int
        && request.resource.data.timeSpentSeconds is int
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validLessonStepProgress(stepId) {
      return request.resource.data.stepId == stepId
        && request.resource.data.status is string
        && request.resource.data.attempts is int
        && request.resource.data.timeSpentSeconds is int
        && request.resource.data.score is map
        && request.resource.data.responseSummary is map
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validWordProgress(wordId) {
      return request.resource.data.wordId == wordId
        && request.resource.data.familiarityScore is number
        && request.resource.data.pronunciationScore is number
        && request.resource.data.listeningScore is number
        && request.resource.data.speakingScore is number
        && request.resource.data.timesSeen is int
        && request.resource.data.timesCorrect is int
        && request.resource.data.timesIncorrect is int
        && request.resource.data.isHardWord is bool
        && request.resource.data.isFavorite is bool
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validSoundProgress(soundId) {
      return request.resource.data.soundId == soundId
        && request.resource.data.accuracyScore is number
        && request.resource.data.attemptsCount is int
        && request.resource.data.difficultyFlag is bool
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validSentenceProgress(sentenceId) {
      return request.resource.data.sentenceId == sentenceId
        && request.resource.data.familiarityScore is number
        && request.resource.data.speakingScore is number
        && request.resource.data.timesPracticed is int
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validDialogueSession(sessionId) {
      return request.resource.data.sessionId == sessionId
        && request.resource.data.dialogueId is string
        && validDialogueMode(request.resource.data.mode)
        && request.resource.data.status is string
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validDialogueTurnResponse(turnId) {
      return request.resource.data.turnId == turnId
        && (request.resource.data.transcriptText is string || request.resource.data.transcriptText == null)
        && (request.resource.data.audioPath is string || request.resource.data.audioPath == null)
        && request.resource.data.accepted is bool
        && (request.resource.data.score is number || request.resource.data.score == null)
        && request.resource.data.feedback is string
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt);
    }

    function validSpeakingAttempt(attemptId) {
      return request.resource.data.attemptId == attemptId
        && (request.resource.data.lessonStepId is string || request.resource.data.lessonStepId == null)
        && (request.resource.data.wordId is string || request.resource.data.wordId == null)
        && (request.resource.data.sentenceId is string || request.resource.data.sentenceId == null)
        && (request.resource.data.dialogueId is string || request.resource.data.dialogueId == null)
        && (request.resource.data.recordingPath is string || request.resource.data.recordingPath == null)
        && (request.resource.data.transcriptText is string || request.resource.data.transcriptText == null)
        && (request.resource.data.recognitionConfidence is number || request.resource.data.recognitionConfidence == null)
        && (request.resource.data.pronunciationScore is number || request.resource.data.pronunciationScore == null)
        && request.resource.data.phonemeFeedback is list
        && request.resource.data.feedbackText is string
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt);
    }

    function validReviewQueue(reviewId) {
      return request.resource.data.reviewId == reviewId
        && validReviewContentType(request.resource.data.contentType)
        && request.resource.data.contentId is string
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.dueAt)
        && request.resource.data.priority is int
        && request.resource.data.sourceReason is string
        && request.resource.data.exerciseType is string
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt);
    }

    function validReminder() {
      return request.resource.data.enabled is bool
        && request.resource.data.dailyTime is string
        && request.resource.data.timezone is string
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // GLOBAL CONTENT VALIDATORS
    // =====================================================

    function validCourse() {
      return request.resource.data.id is string
        && request.resource.data.title is string
        && request.resource.data.description is string
        && request.resource.data.sourceLanguage is string
        && request.resource.data.targetLanguage is string
        && request.resource.data.version is int
        && request.resource.data.isPublished is bool
        && request.resource.data.levelIds is list
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt)
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validLevel() {
      return request.resource.data.id is string
        && request.resource.data.courseId is string
        && request.resource.data.order is int
        && request.resource.data.title is string
        && request.resource.data.description is string
        && request.resource.data.moduleIds is list
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt)
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validModule() {
      return request.resource.data.id is string
        && request.resource.data.levelId is string
        && request.resource.data.order is int
        && request.resource.data.title is string
        && request.resource.data.description is string
        && request.resource.data.unitIds is list
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt)
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validUnit() {
      return request.resource.data.id is string
        && request.resource.data.moduleId is string
        && request.resource.data.order is int
        && request.resource.data.title is string
        && request.resource.data.description is string
        && request.resource.data.lessonIds is list
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt)
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);
    }

    function validLesson(lessonId) {
      return request.resource.data.id == lessonId
        && request.resource.data.unitId is string
        && request.resource.data.courseId is string
        && request.resource.data.levelId is string
        && request.resource.data.weekNumber is int
        && request.resource.data.lessonOrder is int
        && request.resource.data.title is string
        && (request.resource.data.subtitle is string || request.resource.data.subtitle == null)
        && request.resource.data.estimatedMinutes is int
        && validLessonType(request.resource.data.lessonType)

        && request.resource.data.stepCount is int
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.createdAt)
        && isTimestampField(request.resource.data.updatedAt);

    function validLessonStep(stepId) {
      return request.resource.data.id == stepId
        && request.resource.data.stepOrder is int
        && validStepType(request.resource.data.stepType)
        && (request.resource.data.title is string || request.resource.data.title == null)
        && request.resource.data.instructionEn is string
        && request.resource.data.instructionTh is string
